Your role is to execute the tasks created in plan mode.\n\nMODE: BUILD (Thinking ENABLED - you can reason step by step)\n\nIMPORTANT WORKFLOW:\n1. You will receive tasks automatically (from plan mode). Execute each task using available tools.\n2. If you created your own tasks in build mode, call <planDone/> to start executing the first task.\n3. When a task is verified completed, call <nextTask>completed</nextTask>\n6. If blocked, call <nextTask>blocked</nextTask> with detailed explanation\n7. When all tasks done, call <jobDone/> to finish the plan\n\nBLOCKED TASK HANDLING:\nWhen you encounter a blocker:\n1. Call <LogProgress><taskId>ID</taskId><whatWasDone>Attempted X, blocked because Y</whatWasDone></LogProgress>\n2. Call <nextTask>blocked</nextTask> and explain EXACTLY:\n   - What you tried to do\n   - What blocked you (error message, missing file, etc.)\n   - What specific information or action is needed to unblock\n   - What the user should do or provide\n\nAVAILABLE TOOLS (use exact XML format):\n- <Terminal><arg1>ls</arg1><arg2>-l</arg2></Terminal>: Execute terminal commands. Use ONLY for one-liner commands. Params: <arg1>, [<arg2>], ... (dynamic args)\n- <ReadFile><fileName>README.md</fileName></ReadFile>: Read file. Params: <fileName>\n- <WriteFile><fileName>README.md</fileName><contentOfFile># Simple hello world app.</contentOfFile></WriteFile>: Write file. Use for content < 4096 bytes. For larger content, use WriteFile for first chunk then AppendFile. Params: <fileName>, <contentOfFile>\n- <AppendFile><fileName>README.md</fileName><contentOfFile># Second line</contentOfFile><fromLineNumber>1</fromLineNumber></AppendFile>: Append to file. Use for content > 4096 bytes or adding to existing files. Params: <fileName>, <contentOfFile>, [<fromLineNumber>]\n- <CreateFile><fileName>testfile.sh</fileName><contentOfFile># new content</contentOfFile></CreateFile>: Create new file (fails if exists). If file exists and you want to overwrite, use WriteFile instead. Params: <fileName>, <contentOfFile>\n- <List><path>.</path></List>: List files. Prefer this over Terminal ls. Params: [<path>] (optional)\n- <listTools/>: Show all tools. No params.\n- <TreeView><path>.</path><depth>3</depth></TreeView>: Show directory tree. Explore project structure, set depth=0 for unlimited. Params: [<path>], [<depth>] (default 3), [<pattern>] (glob filter), [<showHidden>]\n- <ReadImage><fileName>photo.png</fileName><prompt>Describe this image</prompt></ReadImage>: Read an image file, inject into conversation for AI to analyze (vision model required). Params: <fileName>, [<prompt>]\n- <ExecuteScript><fileName>ls</fileName><args>-l</args></ExecuteScript>: Run script (.py, .sh, .js, etc). Params: <fileName>, [<args>]\n- <Grep><pattern>search_term</pattern><fileName>file.txt</fileName><recursive>true</recursive></Grep>: Search by regex. Prefer this over Terminal grep. Params: <file1>, <file2>, [<unified>]\n- <Sed><pattern>old_text</pattern><replacement>new_text</replacement><fileName>file.txt</fileName><inplace>true</inplace></Sed>: Find/replace. Params: <pattern>, <replacement>, <fileName>, [<inplace>]\n- <ImageTransform><fileName>photo.png</fileName><operation>resize</operation><params>{\"maxWidth\":800,\"maxHeight\":600}</params></ImageTransform>: Transform images (resize, crop, convert, flip, rotate). Params: <fileName>, <operation>, [<params>] (JSON), [<output>]\n- <ReplaceLine><fileName>file.txt</fileName><fromLine>10</fromLine><toLine>20</toLine><replacement>new content</replacement></ReplaceLine>: Replace specific line(s) in a file. Use for targeted edits instead of rewriting the whole file. Params: <fileName>, <fromLine> (required), [<toLine>] (optional, defaults to fromLine), <replacement>\n  **CRITICAL:**\n  - Use <replacement>, NEVER <content> or <contentOfFile>. Wrong parameter causes \"Missing required parameter(s): replacement\".\n  - Always ReadFile first to get correct line numbers (1-indexed).\n  - When replacing a block, include its opening AND closing delimiters in the range.\n  - After ReplaceLine, ReadFile to verify. Multi-line replacements shift later line numbers.\n\n  Examples:\n  Single line:\n  <ReplaceLine>\n    <fileName>config.py</fileName>\n    <fromLine>5</fromLine>\n    <replacement>DEBUG = True</replacement>\n  </ReplaceLine>\n\n  Multi-line block:\n  <ReplaceLine>\n    <fileName>app.py</fileName>\n    <fromLine>10</fromLine>\n    <toLine>15</toLine>\n    <replacement>def new_function():\n      print(\"new code\")\n      return 42</replacement>\n  </ReplaceLine>\n- <Find><pattern>*.py</pattern><path>.</path></Find>: Find by name. Prefer this over Terminal find. Params: <pattern>, [<path>]\n- <Head><fileName>file.txt</fileName><lines>10</lines></Head>: First N lines. Params: <fileName>, [<lines>]\n- <Tail><fileName>file.txt</fileName><lines>10</lines></Tail>: Last N lines. Params: <fileName>, [<lines>]\n- <Sort><fileName>file.txt</fileName><numeric>true</numeric></Sort>: Sort lines. Params: <fileName>, [<numeric>], [<reverse>], [<unique>]\n\nPLAN MANAGEMENT TOOLS (use these to track progress):\n- <planDone/> - Signal planning is done, start the first pending task\n- <nextTask>completed</nextTask> - Mark current task completed, get next task\n- <nextTask>blocked</nextTask> - Mark current task blocked, explain why\n- <LogProgress><taskId>task_id</taskId><whatWasDone>What you did</whatWasDone></LogProgress> - Log progress on current task\n- <viewTask/> - View current plan and tasks\n- <listTasks/> - List all tasks\n- <jobDone/> - Finish the plan (only when all tasks are done or you want to end early)\n- <createPlan><title>Plan Title</title><instructions>Goal description</instructions></createPlan> - Create a new plan (replaces current). Use when current plan needs full replacement.\n- <createTask><title>Task Title</title><instruction>What to do</instruction></createTask> - Add a new task to the current plan. Always create a plan first.\n- <updateTask><taskId>id</taskId><title>New Title</title><instruction>New instruction</instruction></updateTask> - Update a task's title and/or instruction.\n- <deleteTask><id>taskId</id></deleteTask> - Remove a specific task from the current plan.\n- <clearAllTasks/> - Remove ALL tasks from the current plan (keeps the plan itself).\n- <cancelPlan/> - Cancel and delete the current plan entirely (same as deletePlan).\n- <deletePlan/> - Delete the current plan entirely.\n- <deleteDraft/> - Delete the unsaved draft plan.\n- <deleteAllPlans/> - Delete all plans.\n\nTOOL USAGE RULES:\n- NEVER call multiple tool calls for large content. Split large data: WriteFile first chunk -> AppendFile remaining.\n- Prefer targeted edits: Use ReplaceLine for specific line changes and AppendFile for additions instead of rewriting entire files with WriteFile. This is more precise and preserves unrelated content.\n- Prefer XML tools (Grep, Find, List) over Terminal commands (grep, find, ls).\n- For file manipulation with complex data, use WriteFile/AppendFile. For one-liners, echo/cat/tee with Terminal is fine.\n- Use ExecuteScript to run scripts you create (WriteFile/CreateFile). Terminal is for system binaries only.\n- Save useful commands and solutions as tips with <SaveTip>. Retrieve them with <GetTip>. Browse with <ListTips>. Bring saved tips into context with <ReinsertTip>.\n- XML Content: Never use backslashes to escape characters inside XML values \u2014 the parser handles special characters natively. Write raw content without escaping quotes (write `\"Hello\"` not `\"Hello\"`).\n- If a tool returns an error with a \"Usage:\" example, the error message shows the correct parameter names. Copy them exactly \u2014 don't guess. This is faster than trial-and-error.\n\nEXAMPLE WORKFLOW (tasks from plan mode):\n1. Task received: \"Create project folder with basic files\"\n2. Use Terminal to create folder: mkdir myproject\n3. Use WriteFile/CreateFile to create index.html, style.css, app.js\n4. Call <LogProgress><taskId>1</taskId><whatWasDone>Created project folder with 3 files</whatWasDone></LogProgress>\n5. Read back files with ReadFile to verify content is correct\n6. Call <nextTask>completed</nextTask>\n7. Next task is received automatically\n8. Repeat until all tasks done\n9. Call <jobDone/> when finished\n\nEXAMPLE WORKFLOW (self-created tasks in build mode):\n1. Create plan and tasks with createPlan + createTask\n2. Call <planDone/> to start the first pending task\n3. Execute the task using available tools\n4. Call <LogProgress><taskId>ID</taskId><whatWasDone>What was accomplished</whatWasDone></LogProgress>\n5. Verify work with ReadFile/List/TreeView\n6. Call <nextTask>completed</nextTask> when done\n7. Repeat until all tasks done\n8. Call <jobDone/> when finished\n\nBLOCKED EXAMPLE:\n1. Task: \"Install dependency X\"\n2. Attempt: <Terminal><arg1>pip</arg1><arg2>install</arg2><arg3>package-that-does-not-exist</arg3></Terminal>\n3. Error: \"Package not found\"\n4. <LogProgress><taskId>3</taskId><whatWasDone>Attempted to install package-that-does-not-exist, failed with error: Package not found</whatWasDone></LogProgress>\n5. <nextTask>blocked</nextTask>: \"Tried to install package-that-does-not-exist via pip but got error 'Package not found'. User should provide correct package name or installation method.\"\n", "sessionId": 314, "rowId": 0, "timestamp": 1783664760.721038, "date": "2026-07-10"} -->

<!-- {"role": "system", "content": "\nYou are in PLAN MODE. You are architect. Your role is to analyze user requests and create structured task plans.\n\nMODE: PLAN (Thinking ENABLED)\n\nIMPORTANT WORKFLOW:\n\nPHASE 0 - CONTEXT GATHERING (MANDATORY):\nBefore creating ANY plan, you MUST understand the existing codebase:\n1. Call <TreeView><path>.</path><depth>3</depth></TreeView> to see project structure\n2. Call <ReadFile><fileName>README.md</fileName></ReadFile> to understand the project\n3. Call <ReadFile><fileName>AGENTS.md</fileName></ReadFile> to understand conventions\n4. List and read key config files (package.json, requirements.txt, config.py, etc.)\n5. Explore relevant directories with <List><path>src</path></List>\n\nDO NOT create a plan until you've gathered this context. The user may provide files to read directly.\n\nPHASE 1 - CREATE PLAN:\nCall <createPlan><title>Plan Title</title><instructions>High-level goal description</instructions></createPlan>\n\nPHASE 2 - CREATE TASKS:\nCall <createTask><title>Task Title</title><instruction>Detailed instruction for this task</instruction></createTask> for each step\n\nPHASE 3 - FINALIZE:\nWhen all tasks are created, tell user: \"Plan is ready! Type !MODE build to start BUILD mode.\"\n\nHOW TO SPLIT USER INSTRUCTIONS INTO TASKS:\n1. Analyze the user's goal - what is the end result they want?\n2. Identify distinct steps that can be done independently\n3. Create tasks for each step with clear, actionable instructions\n4. Order matters - earlier tasks should enable later ones\n5. Be specific - each task should have a clear beginning and end\n\nTASK SIZE GUIDELINES (CRITICAL):\n- Each task should be completable in 1-5 minutes of AI work\n- A task represents ONE logical unit (e.g., \"Create login form\" not \"Build entire auth system\")\n- If a task requires >3 file edits, split it into smaller tasks\n- Tasks should be independently verifiable\n- Prefer 5-10 small tasks over 1-2 large ones\n- Each task should have clear success criteria\n\nWHY SPLIT INTO TASKS:\n- Easier to track progress\n- Can resume if interrupted\n- Better error handling (failure of one task doesn't affect others)\n- Parallel work possible in future\n\nAVAILABLE TOOLS (use exact XML format):\n- <createPlan><title>Plan Title</title><instructions>High-level goal and context</instructions></createPlan> - Create the plan FIRST\n- <createTask><title>Task Title</title><instruction>Detailed step-by-step instruction for the model to follow when executing this task</instruction></createTask> - Add tasks AFTER creating plan\n- <updateTask><id>taskId</id><status>pending|completed|blocked</status></updateTask> - Update task status\n- <deleteTask><id>taskId</id></deleteTask> - Remove a task\n- <clearAllTasks/> - Remove ALL tasks from the current plan\n- <cancelPlan/> - Cancel and delete the current plan entirely\n- <viewTask/> or <viewTask><id>taskId</id></viewTask> - View plan or specific task\n- <listTasks/> - List all tasks in current plan\n- <TreeView><path>.</path><depth>3</depth></TreeView> - Show directory tree. Params: [<path>], [<depth>] (default 3), [<pattern>] (glob filter), [<showHidden>]\n\nTOOL USAGE GUIDELINES:\n(NOTE: The writing/editing tools below \u2014 Terminal, WriteFile, AppendFile, ReplaceLine, etc. \u2014 are BUILD-mode only. In PLAN mode they will be rejected. Use only plan tools listed above.)\n- Terminal: Use ONLY for one-liner commands. For complex scripts or data processing, use WriteFile/CreateFile.\n- WriteFile / CreateFile: Use for content < 2048 bytes in one call, or when creating a file from scratch.\n- AppendFile: Use when content > 2048 bytes (write first chunk with WriteFile, then AppendFile for rest). Also use for adding new content to existing files \u2014 avoids rewriting the whole file.\n- ReplaceLine: Use for targeted line edits. Specify a single line or a range of lines to replace with new content. Prefer this over WriteFile when you only need to change specific lines.\n  **CRITICAL ReplaceLine rules:**\n  - The parameter is <replacement>, NOT <content> or <contentOfFile>. WRONG: <content>Hello</content> -> ERROR. RIGHT: <replacement>Hello</replacement>\n  - Always ReadFile first to count lines and get exact line numbers (1-indexed)\n  - When replacing a block (CSS rule, function, class), include BOTH the opening AND closing delimiters in the range\n  - Example: to replace a block on lines 15-22, set fromLine=15, toLine=22\n  - After ReplaceLine, use ReadFile to verify the result looks correct\n  - **Edge case \u2014 last block in file**: When editing the final block (e.g. `if __name__ == \"__main__\":`), include the block header in the `fromLine`..`toLine` range. If you replace only the indented body, the header is left orphaned. Example: to replace lines 26-29, use `fromLine=26`, `toLine=29`, and include all 4 lines in `<replacement>`.\n  - If unsure about line range, replace fewer lines and iterate\n  - Multi-line replacement: put raw newlines inside <replacement>...</replacement>. Replacing 1 line with N lines shifts later line numbers by N-1.\n\n  ReplaceLine examples:\n  Single line:\n  <ReplaceLine>\n    <fileName>config.py</fileName>\n    <fromLine>5</fromLine>\n    <replacement>DEBUG = True</replacement>\n  </ReplaceLine>\n\n  Multi-line block:\n  <ReplaceLine>\n    <fileName>app.py</fileName>\n    <fromLine>10</fromLine>\n    <toLine>12</toLine>\n    <replacement>def new_function():\n      print(\"new code\")\n      return 42</replacement>\n  </ReplaceLine>\n- TreeView: Use to explore project directory structure. Set depth=0 for unlimited depth.\n- General Rule: NEVER call multiple tool calls for large content. Split large data: WriteFile first chunk -> AppendFile remaining.\n- Grep / Find / List / TreeView: Prefer these XML tools over Terminal commands (grep, find, ls).\n- XML Content: Never use backslashes to escape characters inside XML values \u2014 the parser handles special characters natively. Write raw content without escaping quotes (write `\"Hello\"` not `\"Hello\"`).\n- EDITING MINDSET: Just as planning splits a big job into small focused tasks, split big file writes into small targeted edits. Use ReplaceLine for specific line changes and AppendFile for additions instead of rewriting entire files with WriteFile. Targeted edits are more precise, safer, and preserve previously written content.\n\nEXAMPLE WORKFLOW:\n1. User says: \"I want a web app with login and dashboard\"\n2. You FIRST create the plan:\n   <createPlan><title>Web App Development</title><instructions>Create a web application with user authentication (login) and a dashboard for logged-in users.</instructions></createPlan>\n3. Then you create tasks:\n   <createTask><title>Setup Project Structure</title><instruction>Create project folder with basic files: index.html, style.css, app.js, server.py. Initialize npm if needed.</instruction></createTask>\n   <createTask><title>Create Backend API</title><instruction>Create server.py with Flask/FastAPI. Add login endpoint /api/login that validates username/password and returns JWT token. Add /api/dashboard endpoint that requires auth.</instruction></createTask>\n   <createTask><title>Build Frontend Login</title><instruction>Create index.html with login form. Connect to /api/login. Store JWT token in localStorage. Redirect to dashboard on success.</instruction></createTask>\n   <createTask><title>Build Dashboard</title><instruction>Create dashboard view. Fetch user data from /api/dashboard with token. Display user info and logout button.</instruction></createTask>\n\nWhen all tasks are created, tell the user \"Plan is ready! Type !MODE build to start BUILD mode.\"\n", "sessionId": 315, "rowId": 2, "timestamp": 1783669398.0916302, "date": "2026-07-10"} -->

Params: <fileName>, [<lines>]\n- <Tail><fileName>file.txt</fileName><lines>10</lines></Tail>: Last N lines. Params: <fileName>, [<lines>]\n- <Sort><fileName>file.txt</fileName><numeric>true</numeric></Sort>: Sort lines. Params: <fileName>, [<numeric>], [<reverse>], [<unique>]\n\nPLAN MANAGEMENT TOOLS (use these to track progress):\n- <planDone/> - Signal planning is done, start the first pending task\n- <nextTask>completed</nextTask> - Mark current task completed, get next task\n- <nextTask>blocked</nextTask> - Mark current task blocked, explain why\n- <LogProgress><taskId>task_id</taskId><whatWasDone>What you did</whatWasDone></LogProgress> - Log progress on current task\n- <viewTask/> - View current plan and tasks\n- <listTasks/> - List all tasks\n- <jobDone/> - Finish the plan (only when all tasks are done or you want to end early)\n- <createPlan><title>Plan Title</title><instructions>Goal description</instructions></createPlan> - Create a new plan (replaces current). Use when current plan needs full replacement.\n- <createTask><title>Task Title</title><instruction>What to do</instruction></createTask> - Add a new task to the current plan. Always create a plan first.\n- <updateTask><taskId>id</taskId><title>New Title</title><instruction>New instruction</instruction></updateTask> - Update a task's title and/or instruction.\n- <deleteTask><id>taskId</id></deleteTask> - Remove a specific task from the current plan.\n- <clearAllTasks/> - Remove ALL tasks from the current plan (keeps the plan itself).\n- <cancelPlan/> - Cancel and delete the current plan entirely (same as deletePlan).\n- <deletePlan/> - Delete the current plan entirely.\n- <deleteDraft/> - Delete the unsaved draft plan.\n- <deleteAllPlans/> - Delete all plans.\n\nTOOL USAGE RULES:\n- NEVER call multiple tool calls for large content. Split large data: WriteFile first chunk -> AppendFile remaining.\n- Prefer targeted edits: Use ReplaceLine for specific line changes and AppendFile for additions instead of rewriting entire files with WriteFile. This is more precise and preserves unrelated content.\n- Prefer XML tools (Grep, Find, List) over Terminal commands (grep, find, ls).\n- For file manipulation with complex data, use WriteFile/AppendFile. For one-liners, echo/cat/tee with Terminal is fine.\n- Use ExecuteScript to run scripts you create (WriteFile/CreateFile). Terminal is for system binaries only.\n- Save useful commands and solutions as tips with <SaveTip>. Retrieve them with <GetTip>. Browse with <ListTips>. Bring saved tips into context with <ReinsertTip>.\n- XML Content: Never use backslashes to escape characters inside XML values \u2014 the parser handles special characters natively. Write raw content without escaping quotes (write `\"Hello\"` not `\"Hello\"`).\n- If a tool returns an error with a \"Usage:\" example, the error message shows the correct parameter names. Copy them exactly \u2014 don't guess. This is faster than trial-and-error.\n\nEXAMPLE WORKFLOW (tasks from plan mode):\n1. Task received: \"Create project folder with basic files\"\n2. Use Terminal to create folder: mkdir myproject\n3. Use WriteFile/CreateFile to create index.html, style.css, app.js\n4. Call <LogProgress><taskId>1</taskId><whatWasDone>Created project folder with 3 files</whatWasDone></LogProgress>\n5. Read back files with ReadFile to verify content is correct\n6. Call <nextTask>completed</nextTask>\n7. Next task is received automatically\n8. Repeat until all tasks done\n9. Call <jobDone/> when finished\n\nEXAMPLE WORKFLOW (self-created tasks in build mode):\n1. Create plan and tasks with createPlan + createTask\n2. Call <planDone/> to start the first pending task\n3. Execute the task using available tools\n4. Call <LogProgress><taskId>ID</taskId><whatWasDone>What was accomplished</whatWasDone></LogProgress>\n5. Verify work with ReadFile/List/TreeView\n6. Call <nextTask>completed</nextTask> when done\n7. Repeat until all tasks done\n8. Call <jobDone/> when finished\n\nBLOCKED EXAMPLE:\n1. Task: \"Install dependency X\"\n2. Attempt: <Terminal><arg1>pip</arg1><arg2>install</arg2><arg3>package-that-does-not-exist</arg3></Terminal>\n3. self.controls[i]\n            if (c.x <= lx < c.x + c.w) and (c.y <= ly < c.y + c.h):\n                return i\n        return -1\n\nclass Toolbox:\n    def __init__(self, x, y):\n        self.x =       \"Dir List\", \"Drive List\", \"File List\", \"Frame\",\n            \"HScrollBar\", \"Label\", \"List Box\", \"Option Btn\",\n            \"Picture Box\", \"Text Box\", \"Timer\", \"VScrollBar\"\n        ]\n\n    def draw(self, stdscr, colors):\n        C_TB = colors['textbox']\n        C_ACTIVE = colors['active_tool']\n\n        write_at(stdscr, self.x, self.y, \"\u250c\" + \"\u2500\" * (self.w - 2) + \"\u2510\", C_TB)\n        write_at(stdscr, self.x + (self.w // 2) - 3, self.y, \"-Tools-\", C_TB)\n        \n        curr_y = self.y + 1\n        write_at(stdscr, self.x, curr_y, \"\u2502\", C_TB)\n        text = (self.items[0] + \" \" * (self.w - 2))[:self.w - 2]\n        write_at(stdscr, self.x + 1, curr_y, text, C_ACTIVE if self.active_tool == 0 else C_TB)\n        write_at(stdscr, self.x + self.w - 1, curr_y, \"\u2502\", C_TB)\n        curr_y += 1\n        \n        write_at(stdscr, self.x, curr_y, \"\u251c\" + \"\u2500\" * (self.w - 2) + \"\u2524\", C_TB)\n        curr_y += 1\n        \n        for i in range(1, 16):\n            write_at(stdscr, self.x, curr_y, \"\u2502\", C_TB)\n            text = (self.items[i] + \" \" * (self.w - 2))[:self.w - 2]\n            write_at(stdscr, self.x + 1, curr_y, text, C_ACTIVE if self.active_tool == i else C_TB)\n            write_at(stdscr, self.x + self.w - 1, curr_y, \"\u2502\", C_TB)\n            curr_y += 1\n            \n        write_at(stdscr, self.x, curr_y, \"\u2514\" + \"\u2500\" * (self.w - 2) + \"\u2518\", C_TB)\n\n    def process_click(self, mx, my):\n        if self.x <= mx < self.x + self.w:\n            if my == self.y + 1:\n                self.active_tool = 0\n                return True\n            elif self.y + 3 <= my <= self.y + 17:\n                self.active_tool = my - (self.y + 2)\n                return True\n        return False\n\ndef write_at(stdscr, x, y, text, attr=0):\n    try:\n        stdscr.addstr(y, x, text, attr)\n    except curses.error:\n        pass\n\ndef draw_properties(stdscr, prop_win, windows, selected_win_idx, selected_ctrl_idx, editing_prop, edit_buffer, colors, tools):\n    C_BG = colors['bg']\n    C_TB = colors['textbox']\n    C_LABEL =   write_at(stdscr, box_x, box_y, \"\u250c\" + \"\u2500\" * (box_w - 2) + \"\u2510\", C_BORDER)\n    for i in range(1, box_h - 1):\n        write_at(stdscr, box_x, box_y + i, \"\u2502\", C_BORDER)\n        write_at(stdscr, box_x + box_w - 1, box_y + i, \"\u2502\", C_BORDER)\n        \n        line_idx = i - 1\n        if line_idx < len(lines):\n            line_text = lines[line_idx]\n            tokens = tokenize_python(line_text)\n            \n            curr_x = box_x + 1\n            chars_printed = 0\n            \n            for text_chunk, ttype in tokens:\n                if chars_printed >= box_w - 2:\n                    break\n                    \n                space_left = (box_w - 2) - chars_printed\n                render_str = text_chunk[:space_left]\n                \n                attr = C_BG\n                if ttype == 'keyword': attr = colors['kw']\n                elif ttype == 'string': attr = colors['str']\n                elif ttype == 'number': += len(render_str)\n                chars_printed += len(render_str)\n            \n            if chars_printed < box_w - 2:\n                write_at(stdscr, curr_x, box_y + i, \" \" * ((box_w - 2)      return None\n        time.sleep(0.01)\n\ndef prompt_input(stdscr, prompt_title, colors):\n    C_BORDER = colors['border']\n    C_BG = colors['bg']\n    C_TB = colors['textbox']\n    \n    box_w =      if len(buffer) < box_w - 5:\n                buffer += chr(ch)\n        time.sleep(0.01)\n\ndef edit_menu_dialog(stdscr, form_win, colors):\n    C_BORDER = colors['border']\n    C_BG =             parent_idx = 0\n                    if cursor < len(form_win.menu_items) and form_win.menu_items[cursor].parent == 0:\n                        write_at(stdscr, box_x + 5, box_y + box_h //                           elif confirm in (ord('n'), ord('N')):\n                                break\n                    form_win.add_menu_item(cap, nid, parent_idx)\n        elif ch == ord('d') or cursor = max(0, len(form_win.menu_items) - 1)\n        elif ch == curses.KEY_UP:\n            if cursor > 0:\n                cursor -= 1\n        elif ch == curses.KEY_DOWN:\n            if cursor <       if c.tool_type != 7:\n            draw_control(stdscr, win, c, i == active_ctrl, colors)\n\n    if active_ctrl >= 0 and active_ctrl < len(win.controls):\n        c = win.controls[active_ctrl]\n        hx = win.x + c.x + c.w\n        hy = win.y + c.y + c.h\n        if hx < win.x + win.w and hy < win.y + win.h:\n            write_at(stdscr, hx, hy, \"\u25a0\", C_HANDLE)\n\ndef draw_control(stdscr, win, c, is_active, colors):\n    C_BORDER = colors['border']\n    C_BG = colors['bg']\n    C_BTN_FACE = colors['btn_face']\n    C_BTN_HL = colors['btn_hl']\n    C_TEXTBOX = colors['textbox']\n    \n    draw_x = win.x + c.x\n    draw_y = win.y + c.y\n    \n    if c.parent > 0 and c.parent <= len(win.controls):\n        parent = win.controls[c.parent - 1]\n        if c.x < parent.x + 1:\n            draw_x = win.x + parent.x + 1\n        if c.y < parent.y + 1:\n            draw_y = win.y + parent.y + 1\n    \n    if c.tool_type == 1:\n        check_state = \"[X]\" if c.checked else \"[ ]\"\n        label = c.caption[3:] if c.caption.startswith('[ ]') or c.caption.startswith('[X]') else c.caption\n        write_at(stdscr, draw_x, draw_y, f\"{check_state}{label}\", C_BG)\n        \n    elif c.tool_type == 2:\n        display_text = c.caption\n        if c.selected_index >= 0 and c.selected_index < len(c.items):\n            display_text = c.items[c.selected_index]\n        if len(display_text) > c.w - 4:\n            display_text = display_text[:c.w - 4]\n        write_at(stdscr, draw_x, draw_y, \" \" + display_text.ljust(c.w - 4) + \" \u25bc\", C_BG)\n        \n    elif c.tool_type == 3:\n        actual_h = max(3, c.h)\n        write_at(stdscr, draw_x, draw_y, \"\u250c\" + \"\u2500\" * (c.w - 2) + \"\u2510\", C_BTN_HL)\n        for r in range(1, actual_h - 1):\n            if r == actual_h // 2:\n                btn_text = c.caption.center(c.w - 2)\n                write_at(stdscr, draw_x, draw_y + r, \"\u2502\" + btn_text + \"\u2502\", C_BTN_FACE)\n            else:\n                write_at(stdscr, draw_x, draw_y + r, \"\u2502\" + \" \" * (c.w - 2) + \"\u2502\", C_BTN_FACE)\n        write_at(stdscr, draw_x, draw_y + actual_h - 1, \"\u2514\" + \"\u2500\" * (c.w - 2) + \"\u2518\", C_BTN_FACE)\n        \n    elif c.tool_type == 7:\n        write_at(stdscr, draw_x, draw_y, \"\u250c\" + \"\u2500\" * (c.w - 2) + \"\u2510\", C_BORDER)\n        for r in range(1, c.h - 1):\n            write_at(stdscr, draw_x, draw_y + r, \"\u2502\" + \" \" * (c.w - 2) + \"\u2502\", C_BG)\n        write_at(stdscr, draw_x, draw_y + c.h - 1, \"\u2514\" + \"\u2500\" * (c.w - 2) + \"\u2518\", C_BORDER)\n        if c.caption:\n            write_at(stdscr, draw_x + 2, draw_y, f\" {c.caption} \", C_BORDER)\n            \n    elif c.tool_type == 10:\n        write_at(stdscr, draw_x, draw_y, \"\u250c\" + \"\u2500\" * (c.w - 3) + \"\u252c\u2510\", C_BG)\n        visible_rows = c.h - 2\n        for r in range(visible_rows):\n            item_idx = c.scroll_offset + r\n            write_at(stdscr, draw_x, draw_y + 1 + r, \"\u2502\", C_BG)\n            if item_idx < len(c.items):\n                item_text = c.items[item_idx]\n                if len(item_text) > c.w - 4:\n                    item_text = item_text[:c.w - 4]\n                if item_idx == c.selected_index:\n                    attr = curses.color_pair(3) | curses.A_BOLD\n                else:\n                    attr = C_BG\n                write_at(stdscr, draw_x + 2, draw_y + 1 + r, item_text.ljust(c.w - 4), attr)\n            else:\n                write_at(stdscr, draw_x + 2, draw_y + 1 + r, \" \" * (c.w - 4), C_BG)\n            write_at(stdscr, draw_x + c.w - 2, draw_y + 1 + r, \"\u2502\u2502\", C_BG)\n        write_at(stdscr, draw_x, draw_y + c.h - 1, \"\u2514\" + \"\u2500\" * (c.w - 3) + \"\u2534\u2518\", C_BG)\n        if len(c.items) > visible_rows:\n            sb_height = visible_rows\n            thumb_size = max(1, (visible_rows * sb_height) // len(c.items))\n            if len(c.items) > visible_rows:\n                thumb_pos = (c.scroll_offset * (sb_height - thumb_size)) // (len(c.items) - visible_rows)\n            else:\n                thumb_pos = 0\n            for r in range(sb_height):\n                write_at(stdscr, draw_x + c.w - 1, draw_y + 1 + r, \n                        \"\u2588\" if r >= thumb_pos and r < thumb_pos + thumb_size else \"\u2591\", C_BG)\n                \n    elif c.tool_type == 11:\n        opt_state = \"(*)\" if c.checked else \"( )\"\n        label = c.caption[3:] if c.caption.startswith('( )') or c.caption.startswith('(*)') else c.caption\n        write_at(stdscr, draw_x, draw_y, f\"{opt_state}{label}\", C_BG)\n        \n    elif c.tool_type == 13:\n        for r in range(c.h):\n            if r == 0:\n                display_text = c.caption\n                if len(display_text) >= c.w:\n                    display_text = display_text[-(c.w-1):]\n                text = (display_text + \" \" * c.w)[:c.w]\n                write_at(stdscr, draw_x, draw_y + r, text, C_TEXTBOX)\n            else:\n                write_at(stdscr, draw_x, draw_y + r, \" \" * c.w, C_TEXTBOX)\n    else:\n        for r in range(c.h):\n            if r == 0:\n                text = (c.caption + \" \" * c.w)[:c.w]\n                write_at(stdscr, draw_x, draw_y + r, text, Hello World (`hello_world.json`)\nA simple introduction to the IDE featuring:\n- Label controls for displaying text\n- Command buttons with click handlers\n- Message box integration\n- Event-driven programming basics\n\n**Usage**: Click \"Click Me!\" to see a greeting, then \"Exit\" to close.\n\n### 2. Calculator (`calculator.json`)\nA functional calculator demonstrating:\n- Grid layout of buttons\n- Text box for display\n- Mathematical operations\n- Event handlers for each button\n- Basic expression evaluation\n\n**Usage**: Click number and operator buttons to build expressions, then \"=\" to calculate.\n\n### 3. Text Editor (`text_editor.json`)\nA simple text editor showing:\n- Multi-line list box for text lines\n- Menu bar with File menu\n- Text input for filename\n- Line manipulation (add, clear)\n- Status bar updates\n\n**Usage**: Use \"Add Line\" to add text, \"Clear\" to reset, select lines to view details.\n\n### 4. Double-click controls to add event handlers\n3. Use the Properties window to customize appearance\n4. Save your project with File > Save Project As...\n\n## Event Types Supported\n\n- `on_click` - Button clicks, menu selections\n- `on_change` - Text changes, check box toggles, list selections\n- `on_focus` - Control receives focus\n- `on_blur` - Control loses focus\n- `on_timer` - Timer intervals\n- `on_load` - Form initialization\n- `on_menu` - Menu item clicks\n\n## Tips\n\n- Use `msgbox(\"text\")` to display messages\n- Access control properties: `controlname.caption`\n- Access list items: `listname.items[index]`\n- Use Python syntax in code editors\n- Test your code in Run mode before saving\n</contentOfFile>\n</CreateFile>", "sessionId": 315, "rowId": 12, "timestamp": 1783671422.3588915, "date": "2026-07-10", "thinking": "", "prompt_tokens": 167031, "response_tokens": 671} -->

<!-- {"role": "assistant", "content": "<CreateFile>\n<fileName>examples/QUICK_START.md</fileName>\n<contentOfFile># VB1-DOS Clone Quick Start Guide\n\n## Getting Started\n\n### Running the IDE\n\n**Python Version:**\n```bash\npython rad-tui-py.py\n```\n\n**FreeBASIC Version:**\n```bash\nfbc rad-tui-BASIC.bas\n./rad-tui-BASIC\n```\n\n### Basic Workflow\n\n1. **Design Mode** (default):\n   - Add controls from the Toolbox\n   - Position and resize controls\n   - Edit properties in the Properties window\n   - Double-click controls to add code\n\n2. **Run Mode**:\n   - Click `[RUN ]` to test your application\n   - Click `[STOP]` to return to design mode\n\n## Controls Reference\n\n| Tool # | Control | Typical Use |\n|--------|---------|-------------|\n| 1 | Check Box | Boolean options |\n| 2 | Combo Box | Dropdown selection |\n| 3 | Command Button | Actions, triggers |\n| 7 | Frame | Grouping controls |\n| 9 | Label | Display text |\n| 10 | List Box | Select from list |\n| 11 | Option Button | Mutually exclusive choice |\n| 13 | Text Box | Text input |\n| 14 | Timer | Periodic events |\n\n## Event Handlers\n\nAdd code by double-clicking controls. Common patterns:\n\n```python\n# Button click\ndef on_click_btnName():\n    msgbox(\"Hello!\")\n    txtDisplay.caption = \"Updated\"\n\n# Text change\ndef on_change_txtName():\n    lblStatus.caption = \"Text changed\"\n\n# List selection\ndef on_change_lstItems():\n    selected = lstItems.selected_index\n    txtDisplay.caption = lstItems.items[selected]\n```\n\n## Property Access\n\nAccess control properties at runtime:\n\n```python\n# Read property\ncurrent_text = txtInput.caption\n\n# Set property\ntxtInput.caption = \"New text\"\nlblStatus.caption = \"Updated\"\n\n# Check box\nif chkOption.checked:\n    msgbox(\"Checked!\")\nelse:\n    msgbox(\"Not checked\")\n\n# List box\nlstItems.items.append(\"New item\")\nlstItems.selected_index = 0\n```\n\n## Menu System\n\n1. In Properties window, click \"Click here to edit menu\"\n2. Press 'A' to add menu items\n3. Set caption and name ID\n4. For submenus, answer 'Y' when prompted\n5. ESC to close editor\n\nMenu event handlers:\n```python\ndef on_menu_mnuFile():\n    msgbox(\"File menu clicked\")\n\ndef on_menu_mnuNew():\n    msgbox(\"New document\")\n```\n\n## Keyboard Shortcuts\n\n| Key | Action |\n|-----|--------|\n| ESC | Cancel / Exit dialog |\n| ENTER | Confirm / Save |\n| Arrow keys | Navigate / Move controls |\n| TAB | Indent in code editor |\n\n## Troubleshooting\n\n**Controls not appearing in Run mode:**\n- Check that controls are within form boundaries\n- Verify control size (minimum 1 height, 4 width)\n\n**Code not executing:**\n- Check function name matches `on_event_controlname`\n- Verify Python syntax (indentation matters!)\n- Use `msgbox()` to debug\n\n**Menu not showing:**\n- Add at least one top-level menu item (parent=0)\n- Menu bar appears below title bar\n\n## Sample Code Snippets\n\n### Counter Application\n```python\ndef on_click_btnIncrement():\n    value = int(txtCounter.caption)\n    txtCounter.caption = str(value + 1)\n```\n\n### Toggle Switch\n```python\ndef on_change_chkEnable():\n    if chkEnable.checked:\n        btnAction.caption = \"Enabled\"\n    else:\n        btnAction.caption = \"Disabled\"\n```\n\n### List Navigation\n```python\ndef on_click_btnNext():\n    current = lstData.selected_index\n    if current < len(lstData.items) - 1:\n        lstData.selected_index = current + 1\n        on_change_lstData()  # Refresh display\n```\n\n## Next Steps\n\n1. Load the example projects to see working code\n2. Modify the examples to understand how they work\n3. Create your own project from scratch\n4. Experiment with different control combinations\n\nHappy coding!\n</contentOfFile>\n</CreateFile>", "sessionId": 315, "rowId": 12, "timestamp": 1783671434.9113479, "date": "2026-07-10", "thinking": "", "prompt_tokens": 167710, "response_tokens": 899} -->

<!-- {"role": "assistant", "content": "I'll create comprehensive documentation for the VB1-DOS Clone project. Let me start with the API reference and other documentation files:\n\n<CreateFile>\n<fileName>docs/API_REFERENCE.md</fileName>\n<contentOfFile># VB1-DOS Clone API Reference\n\n## Controls\n\n### Check Box (Type 1)\nA binary toggle control with checked/unchecked states.\n\n**Properties:**\n| Property | Type | Description |\n|----------|------|-------------|\n| `name_id` | String | Unique identifier |\n| `caption` | String | Label text (prefix with \"[ ]\" or \"[X]\") |\n| `checked` | Boolean | True if checked, False otherwise |\n| `x`, `y` | Integer | Position coordinates |\n| `w`, `h` | Integer | Size (typically h=1) |\n\n**Events:**\n- `on_change` - Fired when checked state changes\n\n**Example:**\n```python\ndef on_change_chkOption():\n    if chkOption.checked:\n        lblStatus.caption = \"Enabled\"\n    else:\n        lblStatus.caption = \"Disabled\"\n```\n\n---\n\n### Combo Box (Type 2)\nA dropdown list for selecting one item from many.\n\n**Properties:**\n| Property | Type | Description |\n|----------|------|-------------|\n| `name_id` | String | Unique identifier |\n| `caption` | String | Default text |\n| `items` | List | String array of options |\n| `selected_index` | Integer | Index of selected item (-1 for none) |\n| `x`, `y` | Integer | Position coordinates |\n| `w`, `h` | Integer | Size (typically h=1) |\n\n**Events:**\n- `on_change` - Fired when selection changes\n\n**Example:**\n```python\ndef on_change_cmbColors():\n    idx = cmbColors.selected_index\n    if idx >= 0:\n        lblResult.caption = \"Selected: \" + cmbColors.items[idx]\n```\n\n---\n\n### Command Button (Type 3)\nA clickable button that triggers actions.\n\n**Properties:**\n| Property | Type | Description |\n|----------|------|-------------|\n| `name_id` | String | Unique identifier |\n| `caption` | String | Button text |\n| `x`, `y` | Integer | Position coordinates |\n| `w`, `h` | Integer | Size (typically h=3 for standard button) |\n\n**Events:**\n- `on_click` - Fired when button is clicked\n\n**Example:**\n```python\ndef on_click_btnSave():\n    msgbox(\"Data saved!\")\n    txtStatus.caption = \"Saved at \" + get_time()\n```\n\n---\n\n### Frame (Type 7)\nA container control for grouping related controls visually.\n\n**Properties:**\n| Property | Type | Description |\n|----------|------|-------------|\n| `name_id` | String | Unique identifier |\n| `caption` | String | Frame title (appears in border) |\n| `x`, `y` | Integer | Position coordinates |\n| `w`, `h` | Integer | Size |\n| `parent` | Integer | Parent control index (0=none) |\n\n**Events:**\n- None\n\n**Example:**\n```python\n# Frame is a container, access child controls directly\ndef on_click_btnInFrame():\n    txtInFrame.caption = \"Updated\"\n```\n\n---\n\n### Label (Type 9)\nDisplays read-only text.\n\n**Properties:**\n| Property | Type | Description |\n|----------|------|-------------|\n| `name_id` | String | Unique identifier |\n| `caption` | String | Display text |\n| `x`, `y` | Integer | Position coordinates |\n| `w`, `h` | Integer | Size (typically h=1) |\n\n**Events:**\n- None\n\n**Example:**\n```python\n# Update label from code\nlblStatus.caption = \"Processing complete\"\n```\n\n---\n\n### List Box (Type 10)\nDisplays a scrollable list of items.\n\n**Properties:**\n| Property | Type | Description |\n|----------|------|-------------|\n| `name_id` | String | Unique identifier |\n| `caption` | String | Label text |\n| `items` | List | Array of string items |\n| `selected_index` | Integer | Index of selected item (-1 for none) |\n| `scroll_offset` | Integer | Scroll position |\n| `x`, `y` | Integer | Position coordinates |\n| `w`, `h` | Integer | Size (h determines visible rows) |\n\n**Events:**\n- `on_change` - Fired when selection changes\n\n**Example:**\n```python\ndef on_change_lstCustomers():\n    idx = lstCustomers.selected_index\n    if idx >= 0:\n        txtDetail.caption = lstCustomers.items[idx]\n```\n\n---\n\n### Option Button (Type 11)\nA radio button for mutually exclusive selection.\n\n**Properties:**\n| Property | Type | Description |\n|----------|------|-------------|\n| `name_id` | String | Unique identifier |\n| `caption` | String | Label text (prefix with \"( )\" or \"(*)\") |\n| `checked` | Boolean | True if selected |\n| `group` | String | Group name for mutual exclusion |\n| `x`, `y` | Integer | Position coordinates |\n| `w`, `h` | Integer | Size (typically h=1) |\n\n**Events:**\n- `on_change` - Fired when selection changes\n\n**Example:**\n```python\ndef on_change_optSize():\n    if optSmall.checked:\n        txtPrice.caption = \"$10\"\n    elif optMedium.checked:\n        txtPrice.caption = \"$20\"\n    elif optLarge.checked:\n        txtPrice.caption = \"$30\"\n```\n\n---\n\n### Text Box (Type 13)\nSingle-line text input field.\n\n**Properties:**\n| Property | Type | Description |\n|----------|------|-------------|\n| `name_id` | String | Unique identifier |\n| `caption` | String | Current text content |\n| `x`, `y` | Integer | Position coordinates |\n| `w`, `h` | Integer | Size (typically h=1) |\n\n**Events:**\n- `on_change` - Fired when text changes\n- `on_focus` - Fired when control receives focus\n- `on_blur` - Fired when control loses focus\n\n**Example:**\n```python\ndef on_change_txtName():\n    if len(txtName.caption) > 0:\n        lblGreeting.caption = \"Hello, \" + txtName.caption\n    else:\n        lblGreeting.caption = \"Please enter your name\"\n\ndef on_focus_txtName():\n    lblStatus.caption = \"Enter your full name\"\n\ndef on_blur_txtName():\n    if len(txtName.caption) == 0:\n        msgbox(\"Name is required!\")\n```\n\n---\n\n### Timer (Type 14)\nTriggers periodic events (simulated).\n\n**Properties:**\n| Property | Type | Description |\n|----------|------|-------------|\n| `name_id` | String | Unique identifier |\n| `caption` | String | Timer label |\n| `x`, `y` | Integer | Position coordinates |\n| `w`, `h` | Integer | Size |\n\n**Events:**\n- `on_timer` - Fired on each timer tick\n- `on_click` - Fired when timer control clicked\n\n**Example:**\n```python\ndef on_timer_tmrAnimation():\n    # Increment animation frame\n    current = int(lblFrame.caption)\n    lblFrame.caption = str(current + 1)\n```\n\n---\n\n## Global Functions\n\n### `msgbox(text, title=\"Message\")`\nDisplays a modal message dialog.\n\n**Parameters:**\n- `text` (String) - Message to display\n- `title` (String) - Dialog title (optional)\n\n**Example:**\n```python\nmsgbox(\"Operation completed successfully\", \"Success\")\n```\n\n---\n\n## Control Access\n\nAccess any control by its `name_id` as a global variable in event handlers:\n\n```python\ndef on_click_btnUpdate():\n    # Read from text box\n    name = txtName.caption\n    \n    # Write to label\n    lblOutput.caption = \"Hello, \" + name\n    \n    # Check check box\n    if chkAgree.checked:\n        lblStatus.caption = \"Agreement accepted\"\n    \n    # Get list selection\n    idx = lstOptions.selected_index\n    if idx >= 0:\n        selected = lstOptions.items[idx]\n```\n\n---\n\n## Property Summary Table\n\n| Property | Applicable To | Read/Write |\n|----------|---------------|------------|\n| `caption` | All | Read/Write |\n| `checked` | Check Box, Option Button | Read/Write |\n| `selected_index` | List Box, Combo Box | Read/Write |\n| `items` | List Box, Combo Box | Read/Write (append) |\n| `scroll_offset` | List Box | Read/Write |\n| `group` | Option Button | Read/Write |\n| `parent` | All (container) | Read/Write |\n| `x`, `y`, `w`, `h` | All | Read-only at runtime |\n\n---\n\n## Event Summary Table\n\n| Event | Triggered By | Applicable Controls |\n|-------|--------------|---------------------|\n| `on_click` | Mouse click | Button, Timer |\n| `on_change` | Value change | Check Box, Combo Box, List Box, Option Button, Text Box |\n| `on_focus` | Receiving focus | Text Box, all interactive |\n| `on_blur` | Losing focus | Text Box, all interactive |\n| `on_timer` | Timer interval | Timer |\n| `on_load` > <contentOfFile># Event Handling Guide
> 
> ## Overview
> 
> VB1-DOS Clone uses an event-driven programming model. Your code runs in response to user actions like clicks, text entry, or timer ticks.
> 
> ## Event Naming Convention
> 
> Events follow the pattern: `on_<event>_<control_name>`
> 
> Examples:
> - `on_click_btnSubmit` - Button click event
> - `on_change_txtName` - Text change event
> - `on_focus_txtInput` - Focus gained event
> 
> ## Event Types
> 
> ### 1. Click...
> (truncated, 8530 chars total)
> </contentOfFile>
> </CreateFile>

<!-- {"role": "assistant", "content": "<CreateFile>\n<fileName>docs/EVENT_HANDLING.md</fileName>\n<contentOfFile># Event Handling Guide\n\n## Overview\n\nVB1-DOS Clone uses an event-driven programming model. Your code runs in response to user actions like clicks, text entry, or timer ticks.\n\n## Event Naming Convention\n\nEvents follow the pattern: `on_<event>_<control_name>`\n\nExamples:\n- `on_click_btnSubmit` - Button click event\n- `on_change_txtName` - Text change event\n- `on_focus_txtInput` - Focus gained event\n\n## Event Types\n\n### 1. Click Events (`on_click`)\n\nTriggered when user clicks a control.\n\n**Controls:** Command Buttons, Timers (when clicked)\n\n**Example:**\n```python\ndef on_click_btnCalculate():\n    # Get input values\n    num1 = int(txtNumber1.caption)\n    num2 = int(txtNumber2.caption)\n    \n    # Calculate and display result\n    result = num1 + num2\n    txtResult.caption = str(result)\n    \n    # Update status\n    lblStatus.caption = \"Calculation complete\"\n```\n\n---\n\n### 2. Change Events (`on_change`)\n\nTriggered when a control's value changes.\n\n**Controls:** Check Boxes, Combo Boxes, List Boxes, Option Buttons, Text Boxes\n\n**Check Box Example:**\n```python\ndef on_change_chkAdvanced():\n    if chkAdvanced.checked:\n        # Show advanced options\n        fraAdvanced.visible = True\n        lblStatus.caption = \"Advanced mode enabled\"\n    else:\n        # Hide advanced options\n        fraAdvanced.visible = False\n        lblStatus.caption = \"Basic mode\"\n```\n\n**Text Box Example:**\n```python\ndef on_change_txtPassword():\n    password = txtPassword.caption\n    \n    # Validate password length\n    if len(password) < 8:\n        lblStrength.caption = \"Weak: Too short\"\n    elif len(password) < 12:\n        lblStrength.caption = \"Medium\"\n    else:\n        lblStrength.caption = \"Strong\"\n```\n\n**List Box Example:**\n```python\ndef on_change_lstCountries():\n    index = lstCountries.selected_index\n    \n    if index >= 0:\n        selected_country = lstCountries.items[index]\n        \n        # Update related fields\n        if selected_country == \"USA\":\n            txtCurrency.caption = \"USD\"\n        elif selected_country == \"UK\":\n            txtCurrency.caption = \"GBP\"\n        else:\n            txtCurrency.caption = \"EUR\"\n        \n        lblStatus.caption = \"Selected: \" + selected_country\n```\n\n---\n\n### 3. Focus Events (`on_focus`, `on_blur`)\n\nTrack when controls gain or lose focus.\n\n**Controls:** Text Boxes, interactive controls\n\n**Example - Form Validation:**\n```python\ndef on_focus_txtEmail():\n    lblHint.caption = \"Enter a valid email address\"\n\ndef on_blur_txtEmail():\n    email = txtEmail.caption\n    \n    # Simple validation\n    if \"@\" not in email:\n        msgbox(\"Please enter a valid email address\")\n        lblStatus.caption = \"Invalid email\"\n    else:\n        lblStatus.caption = \"Email validated\"\n\ndef on_focus_txtPhone():\n    lblHint.caption = \"Format: 555-1234\"\n\ndef on_blur_txtPhone():\n    phone = txtPhone.caption\n    if len(phone) == 0:\n        msgbox(\"Phone number is required\")\n```\n\n---\n\n### 4. Timer Events (`on_timer`)\n\nTriggered periodically for Timer controls.\n\n**Controls:** Timer\n\n**Example - Animation:**\n```python\ndef on_timer_tmrAnimation():\n    # Get current frame\n    try:\n        frame = int(lblFrame.caption)\n    except:\n        frame = 0\n    \n    # Increment frame\n    frame = (frame + 1) % 10\n    lblFrame.caption = str(frame)\n    \n    # Update animation\n    if frame < 5:\n        lblAnimation.caption = \"\u25d0\"\n    else:\n        lblAnimation.caption = \"\u25d1\"\n\ndef on_click_btnStart():\n    # Enable timer (simulated by setting a flag)\n    chkRunning.checked = True\n    lblStatus.caption = \"Animation started\"\n\ndef on_click_btnStop():\n    # Disable timer\n    chkRunning.checked = False\n    lblStatus.caption = \"Animation stopped\"\n```\n\n---\n\n### 5. Load Events (`on_load`)\n\nTriggered when form loads (run mode starts).\n\n**Controls:** Form\n\n**Example - Initialization:**\n```python\ndef on_load_form():\n    # Set default values\n    txtDate.caption = get_current_date()\n    txtUser.caption = get_username()\n    \n    # Populate list\n    lstCategories.items = [\"Electronics\", \"Clothing\", \"Food\", \"Books\"]\n    lstCategories.selected_index = 0\n    \n    # Set status\n    lblStatus.caption = \"Application ready\"\n    \n    msgbox(\"Welcome to My Application!\")\n```\n\n---\n\n### 6. Menu Events (`on_menu`)\n\nTriggered when menu items are clicked.\n\n**Controls:** Menu items\n\n**Example:**\n```python\ndef on_menu_mnuFileNew():\n    # Clear all fields\n    txtContent.caption = \"\"\n    txtFilename.caption = \"untitled.txt\"\n    lblStatus.caption = \"New document created\"\n\ndef on_menu_mnuFileOpen():\n    filename = txtFilename.caption\n    if len(filename) > 0:\n        lblStatus.caption = \"Opening: \" + filename\n        # Load file logic here\n    else:\n        msgbox(\"Please enter a filename\")\n\ndef on_menu_mnuFileExit():\n    msgbox(\"Goodbye!\")\n    # Exit application\n```\n\n---\n\n## Event Chaining\n\nEvents can trigger other events:\n\n```python\ndef on_click_btnLoadData():\n    # This might trigger on_change for lstData\n    populate_list()\n    lstData.selected_index = 0\n    # Manually trigger change event\n    on_change_lstData()\n\ndef on_change_lstData():\n    # Update display based on selection\n    update_detail_view()\n    # Update status\n    lblStatus.caption = \"Data loaded\"\n```\n\n---\n\n## Error Handling\n\nAlways validate data in event handlers:\n\n```python\ndef on_click_btnDivide():\n    try:\n        numerator = float(txtNum.caption)\n        denominator = float(txtDenom.caption)\n        \n        if denominator == 0:\n            msgbox(\"Cannot divide by zero!\")\n            txtResult.caption = \"Error\"\n            return\n        \n        result = numerator / denominator\n        txtResult.caption = str(result)\n        lblStatus.caption = \"Division successful\"\n        \n    except ValueError:\n        msgbox(\"Please enter valid numbers\")\n        txtNum.caption = \"\"\n        txtDenom.caption = \"\"\n        txtNum.focus()\n```\n\n---\n\n## Best Practices\n\n### 1. Keep Event Handlers Focused\n```python\n# Good - single responsibility\ndef on_click_btnSave():\n    if validate_form():\n        save_data()\n        clear_form()\n        msgbox(\"Saved successfully\")\n\n# Avoid - doing too much\ndef on_click_btnSave():\n    # validation + saving + UI updates + logging + email sending...\n```\n\n### 2. Update Status After Operations\n```python\ndef on_click_btnProcess():\n    lblStatus.caption = \"Processing...\"\n    \n    # Do work\n    result = process_data()\n    \n    lblStatus.caption = \"Complete: \" + str(result) + \" items processed\"\n```\n\n### 3. Provide Visual Feedback\n```python\ndef on_change_chkEnable():\n    if chkEnable.checked:\n        btnAction.caption = \"Enabled \u2713\"\n        btnAction.enabled = True\n    else:\n        btnAction.caption = \"Disabled \u2717\"\n        btnAction.enabled = False\n```\n\n### 4. Check the value\n    \n    result = process(value)\n    msgbox(\"Result: \" + str(result))  # Check the result\n    \n    txtOutput.caption = result\n```\n\n---\n\n## Common Patterns\n\n### Master-Detail View\n```python\ndef on_change_lstMaster():\n    index = lstMaster.selected_index\n    if index >= 0:\n        key = lstMaster.items[index]\n        details = get_details(key)\n        \n        txtDetail1.caption = details[0]\n        txtDetail2.caption = details[1]\n        lblStatus.caption = \"Showing details for \" + key\n```\n\n### Wizard Navigation\n```python\ncurrent_step = 0\n\ndef on_click_btnNext():\n    global current_step\n    if validate_step(current_step):\n        current_step += 1\n        show_step(current_step)\n    else:\n        msgbox(\"Please complete all fields\")\n\ndef on_click_btnBack():\n    global current_step\n    if current_step > 0:\n        current_step -= 1\n        show_step(current_step)\n```\n\n### Auto-Save\n```python\ndef on_change_txtDocument():\n    # > <contentOfFile># Project File Format Specification
> 
> ## Overview
> 
> VB1-DOS Clone projects are stored as JSON files with a `.json` extension. The format is compatible between Python and FreeBASIC implementations.
> 
> ## File Structure
> 
> ```json
> {
>   "x": 21,
>   "y": 4,
>   "w": 36,
>   "h": 17,
>   "title": "Form Title",
>   "menu_count": 2,
>   "menu_items": [...],
>   "controls": [...]
> }
> ```
> 
> ## Root Properties
> 
> | Property | Type | Required | Description |
> |...
> (truncated, 5914 chars total)
> </contentOfFile>
> </CreateFile>

<!-- {"role": "assistant", "content": "<CreateFile>\n<fileName>docs/PROJECT_FORMAT.md</fileName>\n<contentOfFile># Project File Format Specification\n\n## Overview\n\nVB1-DOS Clone projects are stored as JSON files with a `.json` extension. The format is compatible between Python and FreeBASIC implementations.\n\n## File Structure\n\n```json\n{\n  \"x\": 21,\n  \"y\": 4,\n  \"w\": 36,\n  \"h\": 17,\n  \"title\": \"Form Title\",\n  \"menu_count\": 2,\n  \"menu_items\": [...],\n  \"controls\": [...]\n}\n```\n\n## Root Properties\n\n| Property | Type | Required | Description |\n|----------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `x` | Integer | Yes | Form X position (screen coordinates) |\n| `y` | Integer | Yes | Form Y position (screen coordinates) |\n| `w` | Integer | Yes | Form width in characters |\n| `h` | Integer | Yes | Form height in characters |\n| `title` | String | Yes | Window title bar text |\n| `menu_count` | Integer | Yes | Number of menu items (0 if none) |\n| `menu_items` | Array | Yes | Array of menu item objects |\n| `controls` | Array | Yes | Array of control objects |\n\n## Menu Item Object\n\n```json\n{\n  \"caption\": \"File\",\n  \"name_id\": \"mnuFile\",\n  \"parent\": 0,\n  \"has_submenu\": true\n}\n```\n\n| Property | Type | Required | Description |\n|----------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `caption` | String | Yes | Menu text displayed to user |\n| `name_id` | String | Yes | Unique identifier for event handling |\n| `parent` | Integer | Yes | Parent menu index (0 = top-level) |\n| `has_submenu` | Boolean | Yes | True if this item has child items |\n\n### Menu Hierarchy\n\nTop-level items have `parent: 0`. Submenu items reference their parent's 1-based index.\n\nExample:\n```json\n{\n  \"menu_items\": [\n    { \"caption\": \"File\", \"name_id\": \"mnuFile\", \"parent\": 0, \"has_submenu\": true },\n    { \"caption\": \"New\", \"name_id\": \"mnuNew\", \"parent\": 1, \"has_submenu\": false },\n    { \"caption\": \"Open\", \"name_id\": \"mnuOpen\", \"parent\": 1, \"has_submenu\": false }\n  ]\n}\n```\n\n## Control Object\n\n```json\n{\n  \"x\": 5,\n  \"y\": 3,\n  \"w\": 12,\n  \"h\": 3,\n  \"tool_type\": 3,\n  \"name_id\": \"btnSubmit\",\n  \"caption\": \"Submit\",\n  \"code\": \"def on_click_btnSubmit():\\\\n    msgbox('Hello!')\\\\n\",\n  \"checked\": false,\n  \"group\": \"\",\n  \"parent\": 0,\n  \"items\": [],\n  \"selected_index\": -1,\n  \"scroll_offset\": 0\n}\n```\n\n### Common Properties\n\n| Property | Type | Required | Description |\n|----------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `x` | Integer | Yes | Control X position (relative to form) |\n| `y` | Integer | Yes | Control Y position (relative to form) |\n| `w` | Integer | Yes | Control width in characters |\n| `h` | Integer | Yes | Control height in characters |\n| `tool_type` | Integer | Yes | Control type (see table below) |\n| `name_id` | String | Yes | Unique identifier for code and access |\n| `caption` | String | Yes | Display text |\n| `code` | String | Yes | Event handler code (may be empty) |\n| `checked` | Boolean | Yes | Checked state (for applicable controls) |\n| `group` | String | Yes | Group name (for option buttons) |\n| `parent` | Integer | Yes | Parent frame index (0 = no parent) |\n\n### Type-Specific Properties\n\n#### List Box / Combo Box\n\n| Property | Type | Description |\n|----------|------|-------------|\n| `items` | Array of Strings | List of options |\n| `selected_index` | Integer | Currently selected index (-1 = none) |\n| `scroll_offset` | Integer | Scroll position for List Box |\n\n## Tool Type Reference\n\n| Value | Control | Default Size |\n|-------|---------|--------------|\n| 1 | Check Box | 20x1 |\n| 2 | Combo Box | 20x1 |\n| 3 | Command Button | 12x3 |\n| 7 | Frame | 20x10 |\n| 9 | Label | 12x1 |\n| 10 | List Box | 20x6 |\n| 11 | Option Button | 20x1 |\n| 13 | Text Box | 15x1 |\n| 14 | Timer | 10x1 |\n\n## Code Encoding\n\nEvent handler code is stored as a single string with escaped newlines (`\\n`).\n\n### Python Format\n```json\n{\n  \"code\": \"def on_click_btnName():\\\\n    msgbox('Hello')\\\\n    txtResult.caption = 'Done'\\\\n\"\n}\n```\n\n### FreeBASIC Format\n```json\n{\n  \"code\": \"Sub on_click_btnName()\\\\n    msgbox \\\\\\\"Hello\\\\\\\"\\\\n    txtResult.caption = \\\\\\\"Done\\\\\\\"\\\\nEnd Sub\"\n}\n```\n\n## Complete Example\n\n```json\n{\n  \"x\": 21,\n  \"y\": 4,\n  \"w\": 36,\n  \"h\": 17,\n  \"title\": \"My Application\",\n  \"menu_count\": 1,\n  \"menu_items\": [\n    {\n      \"caption\": \"File\",\n      \"name_id\": \"mnuFile\",\n      \"parent\": 0,\n      \"has_submenu\": false\n    }\n  ],\n  \"controls\": [\n    {\n      \"x\": 8,\n      \"y\": 3,\n      \"w\": 20,\n      \"h\": 1,\n      \"tool_type\": 9,\n      \"name_id\": \"lblTitle\",\n      \"caption\": \"Welcome!\",\n      \"code\": \"\",\n      \"checked\": false,\n      \"group\": \"\",\n      \"parent\": 0,\n      \"items\": [],\n      \"selected_index\": -1,\n      \"scroll_offset\": 0\n    },\n    {\n      \"x\": 12,\n      \"y\": 8,\n      \"w\": 12,\n      \"h\": 3,\n      \"tool_type\": 3,\n      \"name_id\": \"btnOK\",\n      \"caption\": \"OK\",\n      \"code\": \"def on_click_btnOK():\\\\n    msgbox('Clicked!')\\\\n\",\n      \"checked\": false,\n      \"group\": \"\",\n      \"parent\": 0,\n      \"items\": [],\n      \"selected_index\": -1,\n      \"scroll_offset\": 0\n    }\n  ]\n}\n```\n\n## Validation Rules\n\n1. **name_id uniqueness**: All `name_id` values must be unique within the project\n2. **Menu parent references**: `parent` values must reference valid menu item indices\n3. **Control parent references**: `parent` values must reference valid control indices\n4. **Position bounds**: Controls should fit within form boundaries\n5. **Minimum sizes**: Controls must meet minimum dimensions\n\n## Version History\n\n| Version | Changes |\n|---------|---------|\n| 1.0 | Initial format |\n| 1.1 | Added menu support |\n| 1.2 | Added `code` field for event handlers |\n| 1.3 | Added `parent` for frame containment |\n| 1.4 | Added `items`, `selected_index`, `scroll_offset` for list controls |\n\n## Compatibility Notes\n\n- FreeBASIC and Python versions use the same JSON structure\n- Code syntax differs (FreeBASIC uses `Sub/End Sub`, Python uses `def`)\n- Both versions can load each other's project files\n- Code may need adjustment when porting between versions\n</contentOfFile>\n</CreateFile>", "sessionId": 315, "rowId": 13, "timestamp": 1783671511.1994622, "date": "2026-07-10", "thinking": "", "prompt_tokens": > <contentOfFile># Porting Guide: VB1 DOS to RAD-TUI
> 
> ## Overview
> 
> This guide helps developers migrate applications from the original VB1 DOS (Visual Basic 1.0 for DOS) to the RAD-TUI environment.
> 
> ## Key Differences
> 
> | Aspect | VB1 DOS | RAD-TUI |
> |--------|---------|---------|
> | Language | Basic | Python / FreeBASIC |
> | Platform | DOS | Linux/Windows |
> | UI Style | Text-mode GUI | Terminal-based TUI |
> | File Format | .FRM, .MAK | .JSON |
> | ...
> (truncated, 7190 chars total)
> </contentOfFile>
> </CreateFile>

<!-- {"role": "assistant", "content": "<CreateFile>\n<fileName>docs/PORTING_GUIDE.md</fileName>\n<contentOfFile># Porting Guide: VB1 DOS to RAD-TUI\n\n## Overview\n\nThis guide helps developers migrate applications from the original VB1 DOS (Visual Basic 1.0 for DOS) to the RAD-TUI environment.\n\n## Key Differences\n\n| Aspect | VB1 DOS | RAD-TUI |\n|--------|---------|---------|\n| Language | Basic | Python / FreeBASIC |\n| Platform | DOS | Linux/Windows |\n| UI Style | Text-mode GUI | Terminal-based TUI |\n| File Format | .FRM, .MAK | .JSON |\n| Event Model | Similar | Similar |\n\n## Control Mapping\n\n### Basic Controls\n\n| VB1 DOS | RAD-TUI | Notes |\n|---------|---------|-------|\n| `CommandButton` | `Command Btn` (Type 3) | Same functionality |\n| `TextBox` | `Text Box` (Type 13) | Single-line only |\n| `CheckBox` | `Check Box` (Type 1) | Visual style differs |\n| `OptionButton` | `Option Btn` (Type 11) | Use `group` property |\n| `Frame` | `Frame` (Type 7) | Container behavior same |\n| `Label` | `Label` (Type 9) | Similar |\n| `ListBox` | `List Box` (Type 10) | No multi-select |\n| `ComboBox` | `Combo Box` (Type 2) | Dropdown only |\n| `Timer` | `Timer` (Type 14) | Simulated |\n\n### Not Available in RAD-TUI\n\n| VB1 DOS Control | Workaround |\n|-----------------|------------|\n| `PictureBox` | Use Frame with custom characters |\n| `DriveListBox` | Use Combo Box with drive list |\n| `DirListBox` | Use List Box with directory items |\n| `FileListBox` | Use List Box with file items |\n| `HScrollBar/VScrollBar` | Built into List Box |\n| `Shape` | Use text characters |\n| `Image` | Not supported |\n\n## Property Mapping\n\n### Common Properties\n\n| VB1 DOS | RAD-TUI | Conversion |\n|---------|---------|------------|\n| `Name` | `name_id` | Same purpose |\n| `Caption` | `caption` | Same |\n| `Text` | `caption` | For text boxes |\n| `Value` | `checked` | For check boxes |\n| `List` | `items` | Array of strings |\n| `ListIndex` | `selected_index` | 0-based index |\n| `Visible` | N/A | Always visible |\n| `Enabled` | N/A | Always enabled |\n| `Left`, `Top` | `x`, `y` | Same concept |\n| `Width`, `Height` | `w`, `h` | Character units |\n\n### Event Mapping\n\n| VB1 DOS | RAD-TUI |\n|---------|---------|\n| `Click` | `on_click` |\n| `Change` | `on_change` |\n| `GotFocus` | `on_focus` |\n| `LostFocus` | `on_blur` |\n| `Timer` | `on_timer` |\n| `Load` | `on_load` |\n\n## Code Conversion\n\n### Event Handlers\n\n**VB1 DOS:**\n```basic\nSUB btnCalculate_Click ()\n    DIM num1 AS SINGLE\n    DIM num2 AS SINGLE\n    \n    num1 = VAL(txtNum1.Text)\n    num2 = VAL(txtNum2.Text)\n    \n    txtResult.Text = STR$(num1 + num2)\nEND SUB\n```\n\n**RAD-TUI (Python):**\n```python\ndef on_click_btnCalculate():\n    num1 = float(txtNum1.caption)\n    num2 = float(txtNum2.caption)\n    \n    txtResult.caption = str(num1 + num2)\n```\n\n**RAD-TUI (FreeBASIC):**\n```freebasic\nSub on_click_btnCalculate()\n    Dim num1 As Single\n    Dim num2 As Single\n    \n    num1 = Val(txtNum1.caption)\n    num2 = Val(txtNum2.caption)\n    \n    txtResult.caption = Str(num1 + num2)\nEnd Sub\n```\n\n### Control Access\n\n| VB1 DOS | RAD-TUI |\n|---------|---------|\n| `ControlName.Property` | `controlname.property` |\n| `ControlName.Text` | `controlname.caption` |\n| `ControlName.Value` | `controlname.checked` |\n\n### String Operations\n\n| VB1 DOS | Python | FreeBASIC |\n|---------|--------|-----------|\n| `STR$(num)` | `str(num)` | `Str(num)` |\n| `VAL(str)` | `float(str)` or `int(str)` | `Val(str)` |\n| `LEN(str)` | `len(str)` | `Len(str)` |\n| `LEFT$(str, n)` | `str[:n]` | `Left(str, n)` |\n| `RIGHT$(str, n)` | `str[-n:]` | `Right(str, n)` |\n| `MID$(str, s, l)` | `str[s:s+l]` | `Mid(str, s, l)` |\n| `INSTR(str, find)` | `str.find(find)` | `InStr(str, find)` |\n\n### Message Boxes\n\n**VB1 DOS:**\n```basic\nMsgBox \"Hello, World!\", \"Title\", \"OK\"\n```\n\n**RAD-TUI:**\n```python\nmsgbox(\"Hello, World!\", \"Title\")\n```\n\n### Conditional Logic\n\n**VB1 DOS:**\n```basic\nIF chkOption.Value = 1 THEN\n    txtResult.Text = \"Enabled\"\nELSE\n    txtResult.Text = \"Disabled\"\nEND IF\n```\n\n**RAD-TUI (Python):**\n```python\nif chkOption.checked:\n    txtResult.caption = \"Enabled\"\nelse:\n    txtResult.caption = \"Disabled\"\n```\n\n### Loops\n\n**VB1 DOS:**\n```basic\nFOR i = 1 TO 10\n    PRINT i\nNEXT i\n```\n\n**RAD-TUI (Python):**\n```python\nfor i in range(1, 11):\n    print(i)\n```\n\n**RAD-TUI (FreeBASIC):**\n```freebasic\nFor i As Integer = 1 To 10\n    Print i\nNext i\n```\n\n## Step-by-Step Porting Process\n\n### 1. Export Control Definitions\n\nFrom VB1 DOS, document:\n- Control types and positions\n- Property values\n- Event handlers\n\n### 2. Create RAD-TUI Project\n\n1. Start RAD-TUI IDE\n2. Add corresponding controls from Toolbox\n3. Set properties to match original layout\n4. Adjust positions for character-based grid\n\n### 3. Convert Event Code\n\n1. Copy event handler logic\n2. Convert syntax (see tables above)\n3. Update control access patterns\n4. Test each event handler\n\n### 4. Handle Differences\n\n| Issue | Solution |\n|-------|----------|\n| Graphics not supported | Use text characters or ASCII art |\n| File I/O paths | Use relative paths or full paths |\n| Color differences | Adapt to available color pairs |\n| Font differences | Use standard terminal fonts |\n\n## Example: Porting a Calculator\n\n### Original VB1 DOS\n\n```basic\n' Calculator.frm\nSUB btnAdd_Click()\n    DIM a, b AS SINGLE\n    a = VAL(txtNum1.Text)\n    b = VAL(txtNum2.Text)\n    txtResult.Text = STR$(a + b)\nEND SUB\n\nSUB btnClear_Click()\n    txtNum1.Text = \"\"\n    txtNum2.Text = \"\"\n    txtResult.Text = \"0\"\nEND SUB\n```\n\n### RAD-TUI Version\n\n1. Create form with:\n   - 2 Text Boxes (txtNum1, txtNum2)\n   - 1 Label (txtResult)\n   - 2 Buttons (btnAdd, btnClear)\n\n2. Add code:\n```python\ndef on_click_btnAdd():\n    try:\n        a = float(txtNum1.caption)\n        b = float(txtNum2.caption)\n        txtResult.caption = str(a + b)\n    except:\n        msgbox(\"Please enter valid numbers\")\n\ndef on_click_btnClear():\n    txtNum1.caption = \"\"\n    txtNum2.caption = \"\"\n    txtResult.caption = \"0\"\n```\n\n## Common Pitfalls\n\n### 1. Variable Declaration\n\n**VB1 DOS:**\n```basic\nDIM x AS INTEGER\n```\n\n**RAD-TUI (Python):**\n```python\n# No declaration needed\nx = 0  # Just assign\n```\n\n### 2. String Concatenation\n\n**VB1 DOS:**\n```basic\nresult = \"Hello\" + \" \" + name$\n```\n\n**RAD-TUI (Python):**\n```python\nresult = \"Hello\" + \" \" + name\n# or\nresult = f\"Hello {name}\"\n```\n\n### 3. Arrays\n\n**VB1 DOS:**\n```basic\nDIM items(1 TO 10) AS STRING\nitems(1) = \"First\"\n```\n\n**RAD-TUI (Python):**\n```python\nitems = [\"\"] * 10\nitems[0] = \"First\"  # 0-based indexing\n```\n\n## Testing After Porting\n\n1. **Layout verification**: Check control positions\n2. **Event testing**: Click all interactive controls\n3. **Data validation**: Test with various inputs\n4. **Edge cases**: Empty inputs, maximum values\n5. **Menu testing**: If menus were ported\n\n## Quick Reference Card\n\n```\nVB1 DOS \u2192 RAD-TUI\n\nControlName.Text \u2192 controlname.caption\nControlName.Value \u2192 controlname.checked\nControlName.List(x) \u2192 controlname.items[x]\nControlName.ListIndex \u2192 controlname.selected_index\n\nSTR$(x) \u2192 str(x)\nVAL(x) \u2192 float(x) or int(x)\nMSGBox \u2192 msgbox()\n```\n\n## Resources\n\n- Example projects in `/examples` directory\n- API Reference: `API_REFERENCE.md`\n- Event Handling Guide: `EVENT_HANDLING.md`\n- Project Format: `PROJECT_FORMAT.md`\n</contentOfFile>\n</CreateFile>", "sessionId": 315, "rowId": 13, "timestamp": 1783671534.9933314, "date": "2026-07-10", "thinking": "", "prompt_tokens": 174773, "response_tokens": 2126} -->

Replace with this code:\n\n**Python:**\n```python\ndef on_click_btnAdd():\n    # Get input values\n    name = txtName.caption.strip()\n    phone = txtPhone.caption.strip()\n    \n    # Validate input\n    if len(name) == 0:\n        msgbox(\"Please enter a name\")\n        return\n    \n    if len(phone) == 0:\n        msgbox(\"Please enter a phone number\")\n        return\n    \n    # Add to list\n    contact = name + \" - \" + phone\n    lstContacts.items.append(contact)\n    \n    # Clear inputs\n    txtName.caption = \"\"\n    txtPhone.caption = \"\"\n    \n    # Update status\n    lblStatus.caption = \"Added: \" + name\n    msgbox(\"Contact added successfully!\")\n```\n\n**FreeBASIC:**\n```freebasic\nSub on_click_btnAdd()\n    ' Get input values\n    Dim name As String = Trim(txtName.caption)\n    Dim phone As String = Trim(txtPhone.caption)\n    \n    ' Validate input\n    If Len(name) = 0 Then\n        msgbox(\"Please enter a name\")\n        Exit Sub\n    End If\n    \n    If Len(phone) = 0 Then\n        msgbox(\"Please enter a phone number\")\n        Exit Sub\n    End If\n    \n    ' Add to list (simulated)\n    Dim contact As String = name + \" - \" + phone\n    \n    ' Clear inputs\n    txtName.caption = \"\"\n    txtPhone.caption = \"\"\n    \n    ' Update status\n    lblStatus.caption = \"Added: \" + name\n    msgbox(\"Contact added successfully!\")\nEnd Sub\n```\n\n4. Double-click and add code:\n\n**Python:**\n```python\ndef on_click_btnDelete():\n    idx = lstContacts.selected_index\n    if idx >= 0:\n        deleted = lstContacts.items[idx]\n        lstContacts.items.pop(idx)\n        lstContacts.selected_index = -1\n        lblStatus.caption = \"Deleted: \" + deleted\n    else:\n        msgbox(\"Please select a contact to delete\")\n```\n\n### Add Search\n\n1. <!-- {"role": "assistant", "content": "<CreateFile>\n<fileName>HISTORY.md</fileName>\n<contentOfFile># Version History\n\n## Version 2.0.0 - Major Release (2024)\n\n### New Features\n\n#### Core IDE Enhancements\n- **Save/Load Projects**: JSON-based project file format for persistent storage\n- **Code Editor**: Modal text editor with syntax highlighting for Python\n- **Runtime Mode**: Execute applications within the IDE with live event handling\n- **Toolbox**: 16 control types including new Timer and Frame controls\n\n#### New Controls\n- **Check Box** (Type 1): Binary toggle with checked state\n- **Combo Box** (Type 2): Dropdown selection with items collection\n- **Frame** (Type 7): Container control for visual grouping\n- **List Box** (Type 10): Scrollable list with selection and scrollbar\n- **Option Button** (Type 11): Radio buttons with mutual exclusion groups\n- **Timer** (Type 14): Event-driven timer control\n\n#### Event System Expansion\n- `on_click`: Button and control clicks\n- `on_change`: Value changes (text, selection, toggle)\n- `on_focus`: Control receives focus\n- `on_blur`: Control loses focus\n- `on_timer`: Timer interval events\n- `on_load`: Form initialization\n- `on_menu`: Menu item selection\n\n#### Menu System\n- Menu bar designer with visual editor\n- Support for nested submenus\n- Menu event handlers\n- Runtime menu display and interaction\n\n#### Property System\n- Real-time property editing in Properties window\n- Support for control containment (Frame parenting)\n- Z-order handling for proper rendering\n- Clipping to parent containers\n\n### Improvements\n\n#### User Interface\n- Redesigned Properties window with text-box styling\n- Active control highlighting with resize handles\n- Improved visual feedback during drag operations\n- Status bar in code editor with keyboard shortcuts\n\n#### Runtime Environment\n- Python code execution with globals dictionary\n- Control property access at runtime\n- Message box function for user interaction\n- Error handling with runtime messages\n\n#### Data Management\n- Complete project serialization to JSON\n- Menu structure persistence\n- Control state preservation\n- Cross-platform project compatibility\n\n### Documentation\n\n#### New Documentation\n- `API_REFERENCE.md`: Complete control and property reference\n- `EVENT_HANDLING.md`: Comprehensive event handling guide\n- `PROJECT_FORMAT.md`: JSON project file specification\n- `PORTING_GUIDE.md`: Migration guide from VB1 DOS\n- `TUTORIAL.md`: Step-by-step first application tutorial\n\n#### Example Projects\n- `hello_world.json`: Basic greeting application\n- `calculator.json`: Functional calculator with math operations\n- `text_editor.json`: Multi-line text editor with menus\n- `database_browser.json`: Customer database with navigation\n- `timer_demo.json`: Counter with auto/manual modes\n\n### Technical Changes\n\n#### Architecture\n- Modular control type system\n- Event dispatcher for multiple event types\n- Focus tracking for focus/blur events\n- Parent-child control relationships\n\n#### File Format\n- Version 1.4 JSON schema\n- Support for menu items array\n- Code storage with escaped newlines\n- Type-specific properties (items, selected_index, etc.)\n\n### Bug Fixes\n- Control positioning boundary checking\n- Menu bar click detection\n- Property editing commit handling\n- Runtime mode switching stability\n\n---\n\n## Version 1.1.0 - Enhancements (2024)\n\n### New Features\n- Double-click detection for code editing\n- Property row click-to-edit functionality\n- Toolbox tool selection highlighting\n- Active tool display in status area\n\n### Improvements\n- Smoother drag operations\n- Better mouse coordinate handling\n- Improved redraw performance\n- Enhanced visual feedback\n\n---\n\n## Version 1.0.0 - Initial Release (2024)\n\n### Features\n- Basic form designer with drag-and-drop\n- 5 initial control types (Button, Text, Label, etc.)\n- Properties window for editing\n- Simple event handling (on_click only)\n- Code editor for event handlers\n\n### Controls\n- Command Button (Type 3)\n- Text Box (Type 13)\n- Label (Type 9)\n- Basic layout controls\n\n### self.menu_items = []\n\n    def to_dict(self):\n        return {\n            'x': self.x, 'y': self.y, 'w': self.w, 'h': self.h,\n            'title': self.title,\n            'controls': for i in range(len(self.controls) - 1, -1, -1):\n            c = self.controls[i]\n            if (c.x <= lx < c.x + c.w) and (c.y <= ly < c.y + c.h):\n                return i\n        return    elif self.y + 3 <= my <= self.y + 17:\n                self.active_tool = my - (self.y + 2)\n                return True\n        return False\n\ndef write_at(stdscr, x, y, text, attr=0):\n    try:\n        stdscr.addstr(y, x, text, attr)\n    except curses.error:\n        pass\n\ndef draw_properties(stdscr, prop_win, windows, selected_win_idx, selected_ctrl_idx, editing_prop, edit_buffer, C_BORDER = colors['border']\n    C_BG = colors['bg']\n    lines = msg.split('\\n')\n    w = max([len(l) for l in lines] + [20]) + 4\n    h = len(lines) + 4\n    x = (curses.COLS - w) // 2\n    y = (w - 2) + \"\u2518\", C_BORDER)\n    \n    for i, l in enumerate(lines):\n        write_at(stdscr, x + 2, y + 2 + i, l, C_BG)\n    \n    write_at(stdscr, x + (w - 6) // 2, y + h - 2, \"[ OK ]\", C_BORDER)\n\ndef show_sync_msgbox(stdscr, msg, colors):\n    draw_msgbox(stdscr, msg, colors)\n    stdscr.refresh()\n    while True:\n        ch = stdscr.getch()\n        if ch == curses.KEY_MOUSE:\n            try:\n                _, _, _, _, bstate = curses.getmouse()\n                if bstate & curses.BUTTON1_PRESSED or bstate & curses.BUTTON1_CLICKED:\n                    break\n            except curses.error:\n                pass\n        elif ch in (10, 13, 27) and ch != -1:\n            break\n        time.sleep(0.01)\n\ndef handle_file_menu(stdscr, colors):\n    C_BORDER =        write_at(stdscr, x + 1, y + i + 1, item, C_BG)\n        write_at(stdscr, x + w - 1, y + i + 1, \"\u2502\", C_BORDER)\n    write_at(stdscr, x, y + h - 1, \"\u2514\" + \"\u2500\" * (w - 2) + \"\u2518\", C_BORDER)\n    stdscr.refresh()\n    \n    while True:\n        ch = stdscr.getch()\n        if ch == curses.KEY_MOUSE:\n            try:\n                _, mx, my, _, bstate = y - 1\n                        if idx == 0: return 'save'\n                        if idx == 1: return 'load'\n                        if idx == 2: return 'exit'\n                    return None\n            except curses.error:\n                pass\n        elif ch == 27:\n            return None\n        time.sleep(0.01)\n\ndef prompt_input(stdscr, prompt_title, colors):\n    C_BORDER = colors['border']\n    C_BG = colors['bg']\n    C_TB = colors['textbox']\n    \n    box_w = 40\n    box_h = 5\n    box_x = (curses.COLS - box_w) // 2\n    box_y = (curses.LINES - box_h) // 2\n    \n    buffer = \"\"\n    while True:\n        write_at(stdscr, box_x, box_y, \"\u250c\" + \"\u2500\" * (box_w - 2) + \"\u2510\", C_BORDER)\n        for i in range(1, box_h - 1):\n            write_at(stdscr, box_x, box_y + i, \"\u2502\", C_BORDER)\n            write_at(stdscr, box_x + 1, box_y + i, \" \" * (box_w - 2), C_BG)\n            write_at(stdscr, box_x + box_w - 1, box_y + i, \"\u2502\", C_BORDER)\n        write_at(stdscr, box_x, box_y + box_h - 1, \"\u2514\" + \"\u2500\" * (box_w - 2) + \"\u2518\", C_BORDER)\n        \n        title = f\" {prompt_title} \"\n        write_at(stdscr, box_x + (box_w - len(title))//2, box_y, title, C_BORDER)\n        write_at(stdscr, box_x + 2, box_y + 2, (buffer + \"_\").ljust(box_w - 4)[:box_w-4], C_TB)\n        stdscr.refresh()\n        \n        ch = stdscr.getch()\n        if ch == 27:\n            return None\n        elif ch in (10, 13, curses.KEY_ENTER):\n            return buffer.strip()\n        elif ch in (8, 127, curses.KEY_BACKSPACE):\n            buffer = buffer[:-1]\n        elif 32 <= ch <= 126 and ch != -1:\n            if len(buffer) < box_w - 5:\n                buffer += chr(ch)\n        time.sleep(0.01)\n\ndef edit_menu_dialog(stdscr, form_win, colors):\n    C_BORDER = colors['border']\n    C_BG = colors['bg']\n    C_ACTIVE = colors['active_tool']\n    \n    box_w = 50\n    box_h =
