(box_w - 2) + \"\u2510\", C_BORDER)\n        for i in range(1, box_h - 1):\n            write_at(stdscr, box_x, box_y + i, \"\u2502\" + \" \" * (box_w - 2) + \"\u2502\", C_BG)\n        write_at(stdscr, box_x, box_y + box_h - 1, \"\u2514\" + \"\u2500\" * (box_w - 2) + \"\u2518\", C_BORDER)\n        \n        write_at(stdscr, box_x + 2, box_y, \" Menu Editor \", C_BORDER)\n        write_at(stdscr, box_x + 2, box_y + box_h - 1, \" A=Add | D=Delete | ESC=Close \", C_BG)\n        \n        row = 1\n        for i, m in enumerate(form_win.menu_items[:20]):\n            indent = \"  \u2192 \" if m.parent > 0 else \"\"\n            sel_mark = \"\u25b6 \" if cursor == i else \"  \"\n            text = sel_mark + indent + m.caption\n            write_at(stdscr, box_x + 2, box_y + stdscr.refresh()\n        \n        ch = stdscr.getch()\n        if ch == 27:\n            return\n        elif ch == ord('a') or ch == ord('A'):\n            cap = prompt_input(stdscr, \"Menu Caption\", colors)\n            if cap:\n                nid = prompt_input(stdscr, \"Menu Name ID\", colors)\n                if nid:\n                    parent_idx = 0\n                    if cursor < len(form_win.menu_items) and form_win.menu_items[cursor].parent == 0:\n                        write_at(stdscr, box_x + 5, box_y + box_h // 2, \n                                f\"Add as submenu of {form_win.menu_items[cursor].caption}? (Y/N)\", C_BORDER)\n                        stdscr.refresh()\n                        while True:\n                            confirm = stdscr.getch()\n                            if confirm in (ord('y'), ord('Y')):\n                                parent_idx = cursor + 1\n                                form_win.menu_items[cursor].has_submenu = True\n                                break\n                            elif confirm in (ord('n'), ord('N')):\n                                break\n                    form_win.add_menu_item(cap, nid, parent_idx)\n        elif ch == ord('d') or ch == ord('D'):\n            if 0 <= cursor < len(form_win.menu_items):\n                form_win.menu_items.pop(cursor)\n                if cursor >= len(form_win.menu_items):\n                    cursor = max(0, len(form_win.menu_items) - 1)\n        elif ch == curses.KEY_UP:\n            if cursor > 0:\n                cursor -= 1\n        elif ch == curses.KEY_DOWN:\n            if cursor < len(form_win.menu_items) - 1:\n                cursor += 1\n        \n        time.sleep(0.01)\n\ndef draw_window(stdscr, win, colors, active_ctrl=-1):\n    C_BORDER = colors['border']\n    C_BG = colors['bg']\n    C_BTN_FACE = colors['btn_face']\n    C_BTN_HL = colors['btn_hl']\n    C_TEXTBOX = colors['textbox']\n    C_HANDLE = colors['handle']\n\n    write_at(stdscr, win.x, win.y, \"\u250c\" + \"\u2500\" * (win.w - 2) + \"\u2510\", C_BORDER)\n    title_x = win.x + (win.w - len(win.title)) // 2\n    write_at(stdscr, title_x, win.y, win.title, C_BORDER)\n    \n    for i in range(1, win.h - 1):\n        write_at(stdscr, win.x, win.y + i, \"\u2502\", C_BORDER)\n        write_at(stdscr, win.x + 1, win.y + i, \" \" * (win.w - 2), C_BG)\n        write_at(stdscr, win.x + win.w - 1, win.y + i, \"\u2502\", C_BORDER)\n    \n    write_at(stdscr, win.x, win.y + win.h - 1, \"\u2514\" + \"\u2500\" * (win.w - 2) + \"\u2518\", C_BORDER)\n\n    if win.menu_items:\n        win.draw_menu_bar(stdscr, colors)\n\n    for i, c in enumerate(win.controls):\n        if c.tool_type == 7:\n            draw_control(stdscr, win, c, i == active_ctrl, colors)\n    \n    for i, c in enumerate(win.controls):\n        if c.tool_type != 7:\n            draw_control(stdscr, win, c, i == active_ctrl, colors)\n\n    if active_ctrl >= 0 and active_ctrl < len(win.controls):\n        c = win.controls[active_ctrl]\n        hx = win.x + c.x + c.w\n        hy = win.y + c.y + c.h\n        if hx < win.x + win.w and hy < win.y + win.h:\n            write_at(stdscr, hx, hy, \"\u25a0\", C_HANDLE)\n\ndef draw_control(stdscr, win, c, is_active, colors):\n    C_BORDER = colors['border']\n    C_BG = colors['bg']\n    C_BTN_FACE = colors['btn_face']\n    C_BTN_HL = colors['btn_hl']\n    C_TEXTBOX = colors['textbox']\n    \n    draw_x = win.x + c.x\n    draw_y = win.y + c.y\n    \n    if c.parent > 0 and c.parent <= len(win.controls):\n        parent = win.controls[c.parent - 1]\n        if c.x < parent.x + 1:\n            draw_x = win.x + parent.x + 1\n        if c.y < parent.y + 1:\n            draw_y = win.y + parent.y + 1\n    \n    if c.tool_type == 1:\n        check_state = \"[X]\" if c.checked else \"[ ]\"\n        label = c.caption[3:] if c.caption.startswith('[ ]') or c.caption.startswith('[X]') else c.caption\n        write_at(stdscr, draw_x, draw_y, f\"{check_state}{label}\", C_BG)\n        \n    elif c.tool_type == 2:\n        display_text = c.caption\n        if c.selected_index >= 0 and c.selected_index < len(c.items):\n            display_text = c.items[c.selected_index]\n        if len(display_text) > c.w - 4:\n            display_text = display_text[:c.w - 4]\n        write_at(stdscr, draw_x, draw_y, \" \" + display_text.ljust(c.w - 4) + \" \u25bc\", C_BG)\n        \n    elif c.tool_type == 3:\n        actual_h = max(3, c.h)\n        write_at(stdscr, draw_x, draw_y, \"\u250c\" + \"\u2500\" * (c.w - 2) + \"\u2510\", C_BTN_HL)\n        for r in range(1, actual_h - 1):\n            if r == actual_h // 2:\n                btn_text = c.caption.center(c.w - 2)\n                write_at(stdscr, draw_x, draw_y + r, \"\u2502\" + btn_text + \"\u2502\", C_BTN_FACE)\n            else:\n                write_at(stdscr, draw_x, draw_y + r, \"\u2502\" + \" \" * (c.w - 2) + \"\u2502\", C_BTN_FACE)\n        write_at(stdscr, draw_x, draw_y + actual_h - 1, \"\u2514\" + \"\u2500\" * (c.w - 2) + \"\u2518\", C_BTN_FACE)\n        \n    elif c.tool_type == 7:\n        write_at(stdscr, draw_x, draw_y, \"\u250c\" + \"\u2500\" * (c.w - 2) + \"\u2510\", C_BORDER)\n        for r in range(1, c.h - 1):\n            write_at(stdscr, draw_x, draw_y + r, \"\u2502\" + \" \" * (c.w - 2) + \"\u2502\", C_BG)\n        write_at(stdscr, draw_x, draw_y + c.h - 1, \"\u2514\" + \"\u2500\" * (c.w - 2) + \"\u2518\", C_BORDER)\n        if c.caption:\n            write_at(stdscr, draw_x + 2, draw_y, f\" {c.caption} \", C_BORDER)\n            \n    elif c.tool_type == 10:\n        write_at(stdscr, draw_x, draw_y, \"\u250c\" + \"\u2500\" * (c.w - 3) + \"\u252c\u2510\", C_BG)\n        visible_rows = c.h - 2\n        for r in range(visible_rows):\n            item_idx = c.scroll_offset + r\n            write_at(stdscr, draw_x, draw_y + 1 + r, \"\u2502\", C_BG)\n            if item_idx < len(c.items):\n                item_text = c.items[item_idx]\n                if len(item_text) > c.w - 4:\n                    item_text = item_text[:c.w - 4]\n                if item_idx == c.selected_index:\n                    attr = curses.color_pair(3) | curses.A_BOLD\n                else:\n                    attr = C_BG\n                write_at(stdscr, draw_x + 2, draw_y + 1 + r, item_text.ljust(c.w - 4), attr)\n            else:\n                write_at(stdscr, draw_x + 2, draw_y + 1 + r, \" \" * (c.w - 4), C_BG)\n            write_at(stdscr, draw_x + c.w - 2, draw_y + 1 + r, \"\u2502\u2502\", C_BG)\n        write_at(stdscr, draw_x, draw_y + c.h - 1, \"\u2514\" + \"\u2500\" * (c.w - 3) + \"\u2534\u2518\", C_BG)\n        if len(c.items) > visible_rows:\n            sb_height = visible_rows\n            thumb_size = max(1, (visible_rows * sb_height) // len(c.items))\n            if len(c.items) > visible_rows:\n                thumb_pos = (c.scroll_offset * (sb_height - thumb_size)) // (len(c.items) - visible_rows)\n            else:\n                thumb_pos = 0\n            for r in range(sb_height):\n                write_at(stdscr, draw_x + c.w - 1, draw_y + 1 + r, \n                        \"\u2588\" if r >= thumb_pos and r < thumb_pos + thumb_size else \"\u2591\", C_BG)\n                \n    elif c.tool_type == 11:\n        opt_state = \"(*)\" if c.checked else \"( )\"\n        label = c.caption[3:] if in range(c.h):\n            if r == 0:\n                display_text = c.caption\n                if len(display_text) >= c.w:\n                    display_text = display_text[-(c.w-1):]\n                text = (display_text + \" \" * c.w)[:c.w]\n                write_at(stdscr, draw_x, draw_y + r, text, C_TEXTBOX)\n            else:\n                write_at(stdscr, draw_x, draw_y + r, \" \" * c.w, C_TEXTBOX)\n    else:\n        for r in range(c.h):\n            if r == 0:\n                text = (c.caption + \" \" * c.w)[:c.w]\n                write_at(stdscr, draw_x, draw_y + r, text, curses.mousemask(curses.ALL_MOUSE_EVENTS | curses.REPORT_MOUSE_POSITION)\n    curses.mouseinterval(0) \n    print('\\033[?1003h\\033[?1015h\\033[?1006h', end='', flush=True) \n\n    curses.init_pair(1, curses.COLOR_WHITE, curses.COLOR_BLUE)    \n    curses.init_pair(2, curses.COLOR_BLACK, curses.COLOR_WHITE)   \n    curses.init_pair(3, curses.COLOR_WHITE, curses.COLOR_WHITE)   \n    curses.init_pair(4, curses.COLOR_BLACK, curses.COLOR_CYAN)    \n    curses.init_pair(5, curses.COLOR_WHITE, curses.COLOR_BLACK)   \n    curses.init_pair(6, curses.COLOR_CYAN, curses.COLOR_BLACK)    \n    curses.init_pair(7, curses.COLOR_BLACK, curses.COLOR_WHITE)   \n    curses.init_pair(8, curses.COLOR_BLUE, curses.COLOR_WHITE)    \n    curses.init_pair(9, curses.COLOR_GREEN, curses.COLOR_WHITE)   \n    curses.init_pair(10, curses.COLOR_RED, curses.COLOR_WHITE)    \n    curses.init_pair(11, curses.COLOR_MAGENTA, curses.COLOR_WHITE)\n\n    C = {\n        'border': windows = [\n        Window(21, 4, 36, 17, \"Form 1\"),\n        Window(59, 2, 20, 15, \"Properties\")\n    ]\n\n    selected_win_idx = -1\n    selected_ctrl_idx = -1\n    editing_prop = 0 \n    edit_buffer = \"\"\n\n    mx, my, old_mx, old_my = 0, 0, 0, 0\n    dragged_win = -1\n    dragged_ctrl = -1\n    dragged_tool = False\n    resizing_ctrl = False\n    mouse_down = False\n    drag_offset_x, drag_offset_y = 0, 0\n\n    last_click_time = 0.0\n    last_click_x = -1\n    last_click_y = -1\n    \n    code_mode = False\n    code_lines = []\n    code_cx, code_cy = 0, 0\n    code_target_ctrl = None\n    code_event_type = \"click\"\n    \n    run_mode = False\n    run_globals = {}\n    run_focused_ctrl = -1 \n    design_backup = None\n\n    def commit_edit():\n        nonlocal editing_prop, edit_buffer, selected_win_idx, selected_ctrl_idx\n        if editing_prop > 0 and selected_win_idx >= 0 and selected_ctrl_idx >= 0:\n            c = windows[selected_win_idx].controls[selected_ctrl_idx]\n            try:\n                if editing_prop == 1: c.name_id = edit_buffer\n                elif editing_prop == 2: c.caption = edit_buffer\n                elif editing_prop == 3: c.x = int(edit_buffer)\n                elif editing_prop == 4: c.y = int(edit_buffer)\n                elif editing_prop == 5: c.w = int(edit_buffer)\n                elif editing_prop == 6: c.h = int(edit_buffer)\n            except ValueError:\n                pass \n            c.w = max(4, c.w)\n            c.h = max(3 if c.tool_type == 3 else 1, c.h)\n            c.x = max(1, min(c.x, windows[selected_win_idx].w - c.w - 1))\n            c.y = max(1, min(c.y, windows[selected_win_idx].h - c.h - 1))\n        editing_prop = 0\n\n    def execute_event(event_name, form_win):\n        \"\"\"Execute event handler by name\"\"\"\n        if event_name in run_globals:\n            try:\n                run_globals[event_name]()\n            except Exception as e:\n                run_globals['__msg__'] = f\"Event Error ({event_name}):\\n{e}\"\n\n    stdscr.clear()\n\n    while True:\n        box_w = max(50, curses.COLS - 10)\n        box_h = max(15, curses.LINES - 6)\n        box_x = (curses.COLS - box_w) // 2\n        box_y = (curses.LINES - box_h) // 2\n\n        if code_mode:\n            draw_code_editor(stdscr, code_lines, code_cy, code_cx, code_target_ctrl.name_id, box_x, box_y, box_w, box_h, C, code_event_type)\n            curses.curs_set(1) \n        else:\n            if run_mode and run_focused_ctrl >= 0:\n                curses.curs_set(1)\n            else:\n                curses.curs_set(0) \n            \n            if run_mode:\n                menu_str = \" File  Edit  View [STOP] Debug  Options\"\n            else:\n                menu_str = \" File  Edit  View [RUN ] Debug  Options\"\n                \n            write_at(stdscr, 0, 0, menu_str + \" \" * max(0, curses.COLS - len(menu_str)), C['handle'])\n            \n            if not run_mode:\n                tools.draw(stdscr, C)\n            \n            for i, win in enumerate(windows):\n                if run_mode and i != 0:\n                    continue\n                act_idx = selected_ctrl_idx if (i == selected_win_idx and not run_mode) else -1\n                draw_window(stdscr, win, C, act_idx)\n                if i == 1 and not run_mode:\n                    draw_properties(stdscr, win, windows, selected_win_idx, selected_ctrl_idx, editing_prop, edit_buffer, C, tools)\n\n            if run_mode and run_globals.get('__msg__'):\n                draw_msgbox(stdscr, run_globals['__msg__'], C)\n\n            if run_mode and run_focused_ctrl >= 0:\n                c = windows[0].controls[run_focused_ctrl]\n                display_text = c.caption\n                if len(display_text) >= c.w:\n                    display_text = display_text[-(c.w-1):]\n                try:\n                    stdscr.move(windows[0].y + c.y, windows[0].x + c.x + len(display_text))\n                except curses.error:\n                    pass\n\n        stdscr.refresh()\n\n        ch = stdscr.getch()\n        \n        if ch == curses.KEY_MOUSE:\n            try:\n                _, mx, my, _, bstate = curses.getmouse()\n                mouse_moved = (mx != old_mx or my != old_my)\n                left_click = bool(bstate & curses.BUTTON1_PRESSED) or bool(bstate & curses.BUTTON1_CLICKED)\n                mouse_released = bool(bstate & curses.BUTTON1_RELEASED)\n\n                if left_click:\n                    current_time = time.time()\n                    is_double_click = False\n                    if (current_time - last_click_time < 0.4) and (mx == last_click_x and my == last_click_y):\n                        is_double_click = True\n                    last_click_time = current_time\n                    last_click_x = mx\n                    last_click_y = my\n\n                    if not mouse_down:\n                        mouse_down = True\n                        \n                        if code_mode:\n                            if box_x + box_w - 5 <= mx <= box_x + box_w - 1 and my == box_y:\n                                code_target_ctrl.code = \"\\n\".join(code_lines)\n                                code_mode = False\n                                stdscr.clear()\n                        \n                        elif run_mode:\n                            if run_globals.get('__msg__'):\n                                run_globals['__msg__'] = None \n                                stdscr.clear()\n                            elif 18 <= mx <= 23 and my == 0:\n                                run_mode = False\n                                run_focused_ctrl = -1\n                                if design_backup is not None:\n                                    windows[0] = copy.deepcopy(design_backup)\n                                stdscr.clear()\n                            else:\n                                win = windows[0]\n                                if win.hit_test(mx, my):\n                                    lx = mx - win.x\n                                    ly = my - win.y\n                                    \n                                    # Check menu bar click\n                                    if ly == 1 and win.menu_items:\n                                        menu_x = 1\n                                        for m in win.menu_items:\n                                            if m.parent == 0:\n                                                item_w = len(m.caption) + 2\n                                                if lx >= menu_x and lx < menu_x + item_w:\n                                                    execute_event(f\"on_menu_{m.name_id}\", win)\n                                                    break\n                                                menu_x += item_w + 2\n                                        continue\n                                    \n                                    idx = win.hit_control(lx, ly)\n                                    if idx >= 0:\n                                        c = win.controls[idx]\n                                        \n                                        # Track focus changes\n                                        if not hasattr(win, '_last_focused'):\n                                            win._last_focused = ==========================================================\n\nclass TerminalCompat:\n    \"\"\"Handle terminal differences\"\"\"\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        self.has_utf8 = self._detect_utf8()\n        self.has_mouse = False\n        self.has_colors = False\n        self.term_name = os.environ.get('TERM', 'unknown')\n        \n    def _detect_utf8(self):\n        \"\"\"Detect UTF-8 support\"\"\"\n        lang = os.environ.get('LANG', '') + os.environ.get('LC_ALL', '')\n        return 'utf' in lang.lower() or 'utf-8' in lang.lower()\n    \n    def setup(self, stdscr):\n        \"\"\"Setup terminal capabilities\"\"\"\n        # Check colors\n        try:\n            curses.start_color()\n            self.has_colors = curses.has_colors() and curses.COLORS >= 8\n        except:\n            self.has_colors = False\n            \n        # Check mouse\n        try:\n            curses.mousemask(curses.ALL_MOUSE_EVENTS)\n            self.has_mouse = True\n        except:\n            self.has_mouse = False\n            \n        # Enable UTF-8 if available\n        try:\n            curses.meta(True)\n        except:\n            pass\n            \n        return self.has_colors\n    \n    def get_box_chars(self):\n        \"\"\"Get box drawing characters based on terminal capability\"\"\"\n        if self.has_utf8:\n            return {\n                'h': '\u2500', 'v': '\u2502',\n                'tl': '\u250c', 'tr': '\u2510',\n                'bl': '\u2514', 'br': '\u2518',\n                'tee_r': '\u251c', 'tee_l': '\u2524',\n                'tee_d': '\u252c', 'tee_u': '\u2534',\n                'cross': '\u253c',\n                'block': '\u2588', 'shade': '\u2591',\n                'handle': '\u25a0', 'arrow': '\u2192',\n                'check': '\u2713', 'bullet': '\u25cf'\n            }\n        else:\n            # ASCII fallback\n            return {\n                'h': '-', 'v': '|',\n                'tl': '+', 'tr': '+',\n                'bl': '+', 'br': '+',\n                'tee_r': '+', 'tee_l': '+',\n                'tee_d': '+', 'tee_u': '+',\n                'cross': '+',\n                'block': \"class\", \"if\", \"elif\", \"else\", \"while\", \"for\", \"in\", \n    \"return\", \"pass\", \"import\", \"from\", \"and\", \"or\", \"not\", \n    \"True\", \"False\", \"None\", \"try\", \"except\", tokenize_python(line):\n    \"\"\"Tokenize Python code for syntax highlighting\"\"\"\n    pattern = re.compile(r'(\\s+|\\w+|\"[^\"]*\"|\\'[^\\']*\\'|#[^\\n]*|.)')\n    tokens = []\n    for token in pattern.findall(line):\n        if not token:\n            continue\n        if token[0].isspace():\n            tokens.append((token, 'text'))\n        elif token.startswith('#'):\n            tokens.append((token, 'comment'))\n        elif token.startswith('\"') or token.startswith(\"'\"):\n            tokens.append((token, 'string'))\n        elif token in PYTHON_KEYWORDS:\n            tokens.append((token, 'keyword'))\n        elif re.match(r'^\\d+(\\.\\d+)?$', token):\n            tokens.append((token, 'number'))\n        elif re.match(r'^\\w+$', token):\n            tokens.append((token, 'text'))\n        else:\n            tokens.append((token, 'text'))\n    return tokens\n\n# ==========================================================\n# Core Classes\n# self.checked = False\n        self.group = \"\"\n        self.parent = 0\n        self.items = []\n        self.selected_index = -1\n        self.scroll_offset = 0\n\n    def to_dict(self):\n        return {\n            'x': self.x, 'y': self.y, 'w': self.w, 'h': self.h,\n            'tool_type': self.tool_type, 'name_id': self.name_id,\n            'caption': self.caption, 'code': self.code,\n            'checked': self.checked, 'group': self.group,\n            'parent': self.parent,\n            'items': self.items,\n            'selected_index': self.selected_index,\n            'scroll_offset': self.scroll_offset\n        }\n\n    @classmethod\n    def from_dict(cls, data):\n        c = cls(data['x'], data['y'], data['w'], data['h'], \n                data['tool_type'], data['name_id'], data['caption'])\n        c.code = data.get('code', '')\n        c.checked = data.get('checked', False)\n        c.group = data.get('group', '')\n        c.parent = data.get('parent', 0)\n        c.items = data.get('items', [])\n        c.selected_index = data.get('selected_index', -1)\n        c.scroll_offset = data.get('scroll_offset', 0)\n        return c\n\nclass Window:\n    def __init__(self, x, y, w, h, title=\"untitled\"):\n        self.x = x\n        self.y = y\n        self.w = w\n        self.h = h\n        self.title = title\n        self.controls = []\n        self.menu_items = []\n        self._last_focused = -1  # For focus tracking\n\n    def to_dict(self):\n        return {\n            'x': self.x, 'y': self.y, 'w': self.w, 'h': self.h,\n            'title': self.title,\n            'controls': [c.to_dict() for c in self.controls],\n            'menu_items': [{'caption': m.caption, 'name_id': m.name_id, \n                          'parent': m.parent, 'has_submenu': m.has_submenu} \n                         for m in self.menu_items]\n        }\n\n    @classmethod\n    def from_dict(cls, data):\n        w = cls(data['x'], data['y'], data['w'], data['h'], data['title'])\n        w.controls = [UIControl.from_dict(c) for c in data.get('controls', [])]\n        w.menu_items = []\n        for m in data.get('menu_items', []):\n            mi = MenuItem(m['caption'], m['name_id'], m.get('parent', 0))\n            mi.has_submenu = m.get('has_submenu', False)\n            w.menu_items.append(mi)\n        return w\n\n    def add_menu_item(self, caption, name_id, parent=0):\n        if len(self.menu_items) < 50:\n            self.menu_items.append(MenuItem(caption, name_id, parent))\n            if parent > 0 and parent <= len(self.menu_items):\n                self.menu_items[parent - 1].has_submenu = True\n\n    def draw_menu_bar(self, stdscr, colors, box_chars):\n        C_BG = colors['bg']\n        menu_text = \"\"\n        for m in self.menu_items:\n            if m.parent == 0:\n                if menu_text:\n                    menu_text += \"  \"\n                menu_text += m.caption\n        if       if len(self.controls) < 30:\n            name_id = f\"ctrl{len(self.controls) + 1}\"\n            \n            if ctype == 1:\n                ctrl = UIControl(cx, cy, 20, 1, ctype, name_id, else:\n                ctrl = UIControl(cx, cy, 12, 1, ctype, name_id, ctitle)\n            \n            ctrl.code = \"\"\n            self.controls.append(ctrl)\n            self.redraw()\n\n    def redraw(self, active_ctrl=-1):\n        pass\n\n    def hit_test(self, mx, my):\n        return (self.x <= mx < self.x + self.w) and (self.y <= my < self.y + self.h)\n\n    def hit_control(self, lx, ly):\n        for i in range(len(self.controls) - 1, -1, -1):\n            c = self.controls[i]\n            if (c.x <= lx < c.x + c.w) and (c.y <= ly < c.y + c.h):\n                return i\n \"Option Btn\",\n            \"Picture Box\", \"Text Box\", \"Timer\", \"VScrollBar\"\n        ]\n\n    def draw(self, stdscr, colors, box_chars):\n        C_TB = colors['textbox']\n        C_ACTIVE = colors['active_tool']\n\n        # Top border\n        top = box_chars['tl'] + box_chars['h'] * (self.w - 2) + box_chars['tr']\n        write_at(stdscr, self.x, self.y, top, C_TB)\n        \n        # Title\n        title = \"-Tools-\"\n        write_at(stdscr, self.x + (self.w // 2) - 3, self.y, title, C_TB)\n        \n        curr_y = self.y + 1\n        # First item\n        text = (self.items[0] + \" \" * (self.w - 2))[:self.w - 2]\n        line = box_chars['v'] + text + box_chars['v']\n        write_at(stdscr, self.x, curr_y, line, C_ACTIVE if self.active_tool == 0 else C_TB)\n        curr_y += 1\n        \n        # Separator\n        sep = box_chars['tee_r'] + box_chars['h'] * (self.w - 2) + box_chars['tee_l']\n        write_at(stdscr, self.x, curr_y, sep, C_TB)\n        curr_y += 1\n        \n        # Remaining items\n        for i in range(1, 16):\n            text = (self.items[i] + \" \" * (self.w - 2))[:self.w - 2]\n            line = box_chars['v'] + text + box_chars['v']\n            write_at(stdscr, self.x, curr_y, line, C_ACTIVE if self.active_tool == i else C_TB)\n            curr_y += 1\n            \n        # Bottom border\n        bottom = box_chars['bl'] + box_chars['h'] * (self.w - 2) + box_chars['br']\n        write_at(stdscr, self.x, curr_y, bottom, C_TB)\n\n    def process_click(self, mx, my):\n        if self.x <= mx < self.x + self.w:\n            if my == self.y + 1:\n                self.active_tool = 0\n                return True\n            elif self.y + 3 <= my <= self.y + 17:\n                self.active_tool = my - (self.y + 2)\n                return True\n        return False\n\n# ==========================================================\n# Drawing Functions\n# ==========================================================\n\ndef write_at(stdscr, x, y, text, attr=0):\n    \"\"\"Write text at position with error handling\"\"\"\n    try:\n        if y >= 0 and x >= 0:\n            stdscr.addstr(y, x, text, attr)\n    except curses.error:\n        pass\n\ndef draw_properties(stdscr, prop_win, windows, selected_win_idx, selected_ctrl_idx, \n \")[:10]\n            else:\n                vs = str(val_str)\n                display_text = vs[:10] if len(vs) > 10 else (vs + \"          \")[:10]\n            write_at(stdscr, prop_win.x + 8,            stdscr.move(real_y, real_x)\n        except curses.error:\n            pass\n\ndef draw_msgbox(stdscr, msg, colors):\n    C_BORDER = colors['border']\n    C_BG = colors['bg']\n    lines = \"+\" + \"-\" * (box_w - 2) + \"+\", C_BORDER)\n        for i in range(1, box_h - 1):\n            write_at(stdscr, box_x, box_y + i, \"|\", C_BORDER)\n            write_at(stdscr, box_x + 1, box_y + row >= box_h - 2:\n                break\n        \n        stdscr.refresh()\n        \n        ch = stdscr.getch()\n        if ch == 27:\n            return\n        elif ch == ord('a') or ch == ord('A'):\n            cap = prompt_input(stdscr, \"Menu Caption\", colors)\n            if cap:\n                nid = prompt_input(stdscr, \"Menu Name ID\", colors)\n                if nid:\n                    parent_idx = 0\n                    if cursor < len(form_win.menu_items) and form_win.menu_items[cursor].parent == 0:\n                        write_at(stdscr, box_x + 5, box_y + box_h // 2, \n                                f\"Add as submenu of {form_win.menu_items[cursor].caption}? (Y/N)\", C_BORDER)\n                        stdscr.refresh()\n                        while True:\n                            confirm = stdscr.getch()\n                            if confirm in (ord('y'), ord('Y')):\n                                parent_idx = cursor + 1\n                                form_win.menu_items[cursor].has_submenu = True\n                                break\n                            elif confirm in (ord('n'), ord('N')):\n                                break\n                    form_win.add_menu_item(cap, nid, parent_idx)\n        elif ch == ord('d') or ch == ord('D'):\n            if 0 <= cursor < len(form_win.menu_items):\n                form_win.menu_items.pop(cursor)\n                if cursor >= len(form_win.menu_items):\n                    cursor = max(0, len(form_win.menu_items) - 1)\n        elif ch == curses.KEY_UP:\n            if cursor > 0:\n                cursor -= 1\n        elif ch == curses.KEY_DOWN:\n            if cursor < len(form_win.menu_items) - 1:\n                cursor += 1\n        \n        time.sleep(0.01)\n\ndef draw_window(stdscr, win, colors, box_chars, active_ctrl=-1):\n    C_BORDER = colors['border']\n    C_BG = colors['bg']\n    C_HANDLE = colors['handle']\n\n    # Top border\n    top = box_chars['tl'] + box_chars['h'] * (win.w - 2) + box_chars['tr']\n    write_at(stdscr, win.x, win.y, top, C_BORDER)\n    \n    # Title\n    title_x = win.x + (win.w - len(win.title)) // 2\n    write_at(stdscr, title_x, win.y, win.title, C_BORDER)\n    \n    # Side borders\n    for i in range(1, win.h - 1):\n        write_at(stdscr, win.x, win.y + i, box_chars['v'], C_BORDER)\n        write_at(stdscr, win.x + 1, win.y + i, \" \" * (win.w - 2), C_BG)\n        write_at(stdscr, win.x + win.w - 1, win.y + i, box_chars['v'], C_BORDER)\n    \n    # Bottom border\n    bottom = box_chars['bl'] + box_chars['h'] * (win.w - 2) + box_chars['br']\n    write_at(stdscr, win.x, win.y + win.h - 1, bottom, C_BORDER)\n\n    if win.menu_items:\n        win.draw_menu_bar(stdscr, colors, box_chars)\n\n    # Draw controls - frames first, then others\n    for i, c in enumerate(win.controls):\n        if c.tool_type == 7:\n            draw_control(stdscr, win, c, i == active_ctrl, colors, box_chars)\n    \n    for i, c in enumerate(win.controls):\n        if c.tool_type != 7:\n            draw_control(stdscr, win, c, i == active_ctrl, colors, box_chars)\n\n    # Draw resize handle\n    if active_ctrl >= 0 and active_ctrl < len(win.controls):\n        c = win.controls[active_ctrl]\n        hx = win.x + c.x + c.w\n        hy = win.y + c.y + c.h\n        if hx < win.x + win.w and hy < win.y + win.h:\n            write_at(stdscr, hx, hy, box_chars['handle'], C_HANDLE)\n\ndef draw_control(stdscr, win, c, is_active, colors, box_chars):\n    C_BORDER = colors['border']\n    C_BG = colors['bg']\n    C_BTN_FACE = colors['btn_face']\n    C_BTN_HL = colors['btn_hl']\n    C_TEXTBOX = colors['textbox']\n    \n    draw_x = win.x + c.x\n    draw_y = win.y + c.y\n    \n    # Adjust for parent frame\n    if c.parent > 0 and c.parent <= len(win.controls):\n        parent = win.controls[c.parent - 1]\n        if c.x < parent.x + 1:\n            draw_x = win.x + parent.x + 1\n        if c.y < parent.y + 1:\n            draw_y = win.y + parent.y + 1\n    \n    if c.tool_type == 1:  # Check Box\n        check_state = \"[X]\" if c.checked else \"[ ]\"\n        label = c.caption[3:] if c.caption.startswith('[ ]') or c.caption.startswith('[X]') else c.caption\n        write_at(stdscr, draw_x, draw_y, f\"{check_state}{label}\", C_BG)\n        \n    elif c.tool_type == 2:  # Combo Box\n        display_text = c.caption\n        if c.selected_index >= 0 and c.selected_index < len(c.items):\n            display_text = c.items[c.selected_index]\n        if len(display_text) > c.w - 4:\n            display_text = display_text[:c.w - 4]\n        write_at(stdscr, draw_x, draw_y, \" \" + display_text.ljust(c.w - 4) + \" [v]\", C_BG)\n        \n    elif c.tool_type == 3:  # Command Button\n        actual_h = max(3, c.h)\n        top = box_chars['tl'] + box_chars['h'] * (c.w - 2) + box_chars['tr']\n        write_at(stdscr, draw_x, draw_y, top, C_BTN_HL)\n        for r in range(1, actual_h - 1):\n            if r == actual_h // 2:\n                btn_text = c.caption.center(c.w - 2)\n                line = box_chars['v'] + btn_text + box_chars['v']\n                write_at(stdscr, draw_x, draw_y + r, line, C_BTN_FACE)\n            else:\n                line = box_chars['v'] + \" \" * (c.w - 2) + box_chars['v']\n                write_at(stdscr, draw_x, draw_y + r, line, C_BTN_FACE)\n        bottom = box_chars['bl'] + box_chars['h'] * (c.w - 2) + box_chars['br']\n        write_at(stdscr, draw_x, draw_y + actual_h - 1, bottom, C_BTN_FACE)\n        \n    elif c.tool_type == 7:  # Frame\n        top = box_chars['tl'] + box_chars['h'] * (c.w - 2) + box_chars['tr']\n        write_at(stdscr, draw_x, draw_y, top, C_BORDER)\n        for r in range(1, c.h - 1):\n            line = box_chars['v'] + \" \" * (c.w - 2) + box_chars['v']\n            write_at(stdscr, draw_x, draw_y + r, line, C_BG)\n        bottom = box_chars['bl'] + box_chars['h'] * (c.w - 2) + box_chars['br']\n        write_at(stdscr, draw_x, draw_y + c.h - 1, bottom, C_BORDER)\n        if c.caption:\n            write_at(stdscr, draw_x + 2, draw_y, f\" {c.caption} \", C_BORDER)\n            \n    elif c.tool_type == 10:  # List Box\n        top = box_chars['tl'] + box_chars['h'] * (c.w - 3) + box_chars['tee_d'] + box_chars['tr']\n        write_at(stdscr, draw_x, draw_y, top, C_BG)\n        visible_rows = c.h - 2\n        for r in range(visible_rows):\n            item_idx = c.scroll_offset + r\n            line = box_chars['v']\n            if item_idx < len(c.items):\n                item_text = c.items[item_idx]\n                if len(item_text) > c.w - 4:\n                    item_text = item_text[:c.w - 4]\n                if item_idx == c.selected_index and TERM.has_colors:\n                    attr = curses.color_pair(3) | curses.A_BOLD\n                else:\n                    attr = C_BG\n                line += \" \" + item_text.ljust(c.w - 4)[:c.w-4]\n            else:\n                line += \" \" * (c.w - 3)\n            line += box_chars['v'] + box_chars['v']\n            write_at(stdscr, draw_x, draw_y + 1 + r, line, attr if item_idx == c.selected_index and TERM.has_colors else C_BG)\n        \n        bottom = box_chars['bl'] + box_chars['h'] * (c.w - 3) + box_chars['tee_u'] + box_chars['br']\n        write_at(stdscr, draw_x, draw_y + c.h - 1, bottom, C_BG)\n        \n        # Scrollbar\n        if len(c.items) > visible_rows:\n            sb_height = visible_rows\n            thumb_size = max(1, (visible_rows * sb_height) // len(c.items))\n            if len(c.items) > visible_rows:\n                thumb_pos = (c.scroll_offset * (sb_height - thumb_size)) // (len(c.items) - visible_rows)\n            else:\n                thumb_pos = 0\n            for r in range(sb_height):\n                ch = box_chars['block'] if r >= thumb_pos and r < thumb_pos + thumb_size else box_chars['shade']\n                write_at(stdscr, draw_x + c.w - 1, draw_y + 1 + r, ch, C_BG)\n                \n    elif c.tool_type == 11:  # Option Button\n        opt_state = \"(*)\" if c.checked else \"( )\"\n        label = c.caption[3:] if c.caption.startswith('( )') or c.caption.startswith('(*)') else c.caption\n        write_at(stdscr, draw_x, draw_y, f\"{opt_state}{label}\", C_BG)\n        \n    elif c.tool_type == 13:  # Text Box\n        for r in range(c.h):\n            if r == 0:\n                display_text = c.caption\n                if len(display_text) >= c.w:\n                    display_text = display_text[-(c.w-1):]\n                text = (display_text + \" \" * c.w)[:c.w]\n                write_at(stdscr, draw_x, draw_y + r, text, C_TEXTBOX)\n            else:\n                write_at(stdscr, draw_x, draw_y + r, \" \" * c.w, C_TEXTBOX)\n    else:\n        for r in range(c.h):\n            if r == 0:\n                text = (c.caption + \" \" * c.w)[:c.w]\n                write_at(stdscr, draw_x, draw_y + r, text, C_TEXTBOX)\n            else:\n                write_at(stdscr, draw_x, draw_y + r, \" \" * c.w, C_TEXTBOX)\n\n# ==========================================================\n# Main Application\n# ==========================================================\n\ndef main(stdscr):\n    # Initialize terminal compatibility\n    TERM.setup(stdscr)\n    box_chars = TERM.get_box_chars()\n    \n    curses.curs_set(0)\n    stdscr.nodelay(True)\n    \n    # Setup mouse with error handling\n    try:\n        curses.mousemask(curses.ALL_MOUSE_EVENTS | curses.REPORT_MOUSE_POSITION)\n        curses.mouseinterval(0)\n        # Enable extended mouse mode\n        print('\\033[?1003h\\033[?1015h\\033[?1006h', end='', flush=True)\n        TERM.has_mouse = True\n    except Exception as e:\n        TERM.has_mouse = False\n        print(f\"Mouse setup warning: {e}\", file=sys.stderr)\n\n    # Initialize colors if available\n    if TERM.has_colors:\n        curses.init_pair(1, curses.COLOR_WHITE, curses.COLOR_BLUE)    \n        curses.init_pair(2, curses.COLOR_BLACK, curses.COLOR_WHITE)   \n        curses.init_pair(3, curses.COLOR_WHITE, curses.COLOR_WHITE)   \n        curses.init_pair(4, curses.COLOR_BLACK, curses.COLOR_CYAN)    \n        curses.init_pair(5, curses.COLOR_WHITE, curses.COLOR_BLACK)   \n        curses.init_pair(6, curses.COLOR_CYAN, curses.COLOR_BLACK)    \n        curses.init_pair(7, curses.COLOR_BLACK, curses.COLOR_WHITE)   \n        curses.init_pair(8, curses.COLOR_BLUE, curses.COLOR_WHITE)    \n        curses.init_pair(9, curses.COLOR_GREEN, curses.COLOR_WHITE)   \n        curses.init_pair(10, curses.COLOR_RED, curses.COLOR_WHITE)    \n        curses.init_pair(11, curses.COLOR_MAGENTA, curses.COLOR_WHITE)\n\n        C = {\n            'border': curses.color_pair(1) | curses.A_BOLD,\n            'bg': curses.color_pair(2),\n            'btn_face': curses.color_pair(2),\n            'btn_hl': curses.color_pair(3) | curses.A_BOLD,\n            'textbox': curses.color_pair(4),\n            'handle': curses.color_pair(5),\n            'active_tool': curses.color_pair(6) | curses.A_BOLD,\n            'prop_label': curses.color_pair(7),\n            'kw': curses.color_pair(8) | curses.A_BOLD,\n            'str': curses.color_pair(9),\n            'comment': curses.color_pair(10),\n            'num': curses.color_pair(11)\n        }\n    else:\n        # Monochrome fallback\n        C = {\n            'border': curses.A_BOLD,\n            'bg': 0,\n            'btn_face': 0,\n            'btn_hl': curses.A_BOLD,\n            'textbox': curses.A_REVERSE,\n            'handle': curses.A_BOLD,\n            'active_tool': curses.A_BOLD,\n            'prop_label': 0,\n            'kw': curses.A_BOLD,\n            'str': 0,\n            'comment': curses.A_DIM,\n            'num': 0\n        }\n\n    tools = Toolbox(1, 2)\n    windows = [\n        Window(21, 4, 36, 17, \"Form 1\"),\n        Window(59, 2, 20, 15, \"Properties\")\n    ]\n\n    selected_win_idx = -1\n    selected_ctrl_idx = -1\n    editing_prop = 0 \n    edit_buffer = \"\"\n\n    mx, my, old_mx, old_my = 0, 0, 0, 0\n    dragged_win = -1\n    dragged_ctrl = -1\n    dragged_tool = False\n    resizing_ctrl = False\n    mouse_down = False\n    drag_offset_x, drag_offset_y = 0, 0\n\n    last_click_time = 0.0\n    last_click_x = -1\n    last_click_y = -1\n    \n    code_mode = False\n    code_lines = []\n    code_cx, code_cy = 0, 0\n    code_target_ctrl = None\n    code_event_type = \"click\"\n    \n    run_mode = False\n    run_globals = {}\n    run_focused_ctrl = -1 \n    design_backup = None\n\n    def commit_edit():\n        nonlocal editing_prop, edit_buffer, selected_win_idx, selected_ctrl_idx\n        if editing_prop > 0 and selected_win_idx >= 0 and selected_ctrl_idx >= 0:\n            c = windows[selected_win_idx].controls[selected_ctrl_idx]\n            try:\n                if editing_prop == 1: c.name_id = edit_buffer\n                elif editing_prop == 2: c.caption = edit_buffer\n                elif editing_prop == 3: c.x = int(edit_buffer)\n                elif editing_prop == 4: c.y = int(edit_buffer)\n                elif editing_prop == 5: c.w = int(edit_buffer)\n                elif editing_prop == 6: c.h = int(edit_buffer)\n            except ValueError:\n                pass \n            c.w = max(4, c.w)\n            c.h = max(3 if c.tool_type == 3 else 1, c.h)\n            c.x = max(1, min(c.x, windows[selected_win_idx].w - c.w - 1))\n            c.y = max(1, min(c.y, windows[selected_win_idx].h - c.h - 1))\n        editing_prop = 0\n\n    def execute_event(event_name, form_win):\n        \"\"\"Execute event handler by name\"\"\"\n        if event_name in run_globals:\n            try:\n                run_globals[event_name]()\n            except Exception as e:\n                run_globals['__msg__'] = f\"Event Error ({event_name}):\\n{e}\"\n\n    stdscr.clear()\n\n    # Main loop with frame rate limiting\n    last_draw = 0\n    frame_delay = 1/30  # 30 FPS max\n    \n    while True:\n        current_time = time.time()\n        \n        # Calculate dialog dimensions\n        box_w = max(50, curses.COLS - 10)\n        box_h = max(15, curses.LINES - 6)\n        box_x = (curses.COLS - box_w) // 2\n        box_y = (curses.LINES - box_h) // 2\n\n        # Draw only when needed or at frame rate\n        if current_time - last_draw >= frame_delay or code_mode:\n            if code_mode:\n                draw_code_editor(stdscr, code_lines, code_cy, code_cx, \n                               code_target_ctrl.name_id, box_x, box_y, \n                               box_w, box_h, C, code_event_type)\n                curses.curs_set(1) \n            else:\n                if run_mode and run_focused_ctrl >= 0:\n                    curses.curs_set(1)\n                else:\n                    curses.curs_set(0) \n                \n                # Menu bar\n                if run_mode:\n                    menu_str = \" File  Edit  View [STOP] Debug  Options\"\n                else:\n                    menu_str = \" File  Edit  View [RUN ] Debug  Options\"\n                    \n                write_at(stdscr, 0, 0, menu_str + \" \" * max(0, curses.COLS - len(menu_str)), C['handle'])\n                \n                if not run_mode:\n                    tools.draw(stdscr, C, box_chars)\n                \n                for i, win in enumerate(windows):\n                    if run_mode and i != 0:\n                        continue\n                    act_idx = selected_ctrl_idx if (i == selected_win_idx and not run_mode) else -1\n                    draw_window(stdscr, win, C, box_chars, act_idx)\n                    if i == 1 and not run_mode:\n                        draw_properties(stdscr, win, windows, selected_win_idx, \n                                     selected_ctrl_idx, editing_prop, edit_buffer, C, tools)\n\n                if run_mode and run_globals.get('__msg__'):\n                    draw_msgbox(stdscr, run_globals['__msg__'], C)\n\n                if run_mode and run_focused_ctrl >= 0:\n                    c = windows[0].controls[run_focused_ctrl]\n                    display_text = c.caption\n                    if len(display_text) >= c.w:\n                        display_text = display_text[-(c.w-1):]\n                    try:\n                        stdscr.move(windows[0].y + c.y, windows[0].x + c.x + len(display_text))\n                    except curses.error:\n                        pass\n\n            stdscr.refresh()\n            last_draw = current_time\n\n        # Input handling\n        ch = stdscr.getch()\n        \n        if ch == curses.KEY_MOUSE and TERM.has_mouse:\n            try:\n                _, mx, my, _, bstate = curses.getmouse()\n                mouse_moved = (mx != old_mx or my != old_my)\n                left_click = bool(bstate & curses.BUTTON1_PRESSED) or bool(bstate & curses.BUTTON1_CLICKED)\n                mouse_released = bool(bstate & curses.BUTTON1_RELEASED)\n\n                if left_click:\n                    current_time = time.time()\n                    is_double_click = False\n                    if (current_time - last_click_time < 0.4) and (mx == last_click_x and my == last_click_y):\n                        is_double_click = True\n                    last_click_time = current_time\n                    last_click_x = mx\n                    last_click_y = my\n\n                    if not mouse_down:\n                        mouse_down = True\n                        \n                        if code_mode:\n                            if box_x + box_w - 5 <= mx <= box_x + box_w - 1 and my == box_y:\n                                code_target_ctrl.code = \"\\n\".join(code_lines)\n                                code_mode = False\n                                stdscr.clear()\n                        \n                        elif run_mode:\n                            if run_globals.get('__msg__'):\n                                run_globals['__msg__'] = None \n                                stdscr.clear()\n                            elif 18 <= mx <= 23 and my == 0:\n                                run_mode = False\n                                run_focused_ctrl = -1\n                                if design_backup is not None:\n                                    windows[0] = copy.deepcopy(design_backup)\n                                stdscr.clear()\n                            else:\n                                win = windows[0]\n                                if win.hit_test(mx, my):\n                                    lx = mx - win.x\n                                    ly = my - win.y\n                                    \n                                    # Check menu bar click\n                                    if ly == 1 and win.menu_items:\n                                        menu_x = 1\n                                        for m in win.menu_items:\n                                            if m.parent == 0:\n                                                item_w = len(m.caption) + 2\n                                                if lx >= menu_x and lx < menu_x + item_w:\n                                                    execute_event(f\"on_menu_{m.name_id}\", win)\n                                                    break\n                                                menu_x += item_w + 2\n                                        continue\n                                    \n                                    idx = win.hit_control(lx, ly)\n                                    if idx >= 0:\n                                        c = win.controls[idx]\n                                        \n                                        # Track focus changes\n                                        if idx != win._last_focused:\n                                            if win._last_focused >= 0:\n                                                last_c = win.controls[win._last_focused]\n                                                execute_event(f\"on_blur_{last_c.name_id}\", win)\n                                            execute_event(f\"on_focus_{c.name_id}\", win)\n                                            win._last_focused = idx\n                                        \n                                        if c.tool_type == 1:\n                                            c.checked = not c.checked\n                                            execute_event(f\"on_change_{c.name_id}\", win)\n                                            win.redraw()\n                                        elif c.tool_type == 2:\n                                            c.selected_index += 1\n                                            if c.selected_index >= len(c.items):\n                                                c.selected_index = 0\n                                            execute_event(f\"on_change_{c.name_id}\", win)\n                                            win.redraw()\n                                        elif c.tool_type == 3:\n                                            execute_event(f\"on_click_{c.name_id}\", win)\n                                            win.redraw()\n                                        elif c.tool_type == 10:\n                                            rel_y = ly - c.y - 1\n                                            item_idx = c.scroll_offset + rel_y\n                                            if 0 <= item_idx < len(c.items):\n                                                c.selected_index = item_idx\n                                                execute_event(f\"on_change_{c.name_id}\", win)\n                                            win.redraw()\n                                        elif c.tool_type == 11:\n                                            c.checked = True\n                                            for other in win.controls:\n                                                if other.tool_type == 11 and other != c and other.group == c.group:\n                                                    other.checked = False\n                                            execute_event(f\"on_change_{c.name_id}\", win)\n                                            win.redraw()\n                                        elif c.tool_type == 13:\n                                            run_focused_ctrl = idx\n                                            execute_event(f\"on_focus_{c.name_id}\", win)\n                                    else:\n                                        if win._last_focused >= 0:\n                                            last_c = win.controls[win._last_focused]\n                                            execute_event(f\"on_blur_{last_c.name_id}\", win)\n                                            win._last_focused = -1\n                        \n                        else:\n                            # Design mode mouse handling\n                            clicked_handled = False\n                            prop_win = windows[1]\n                            prop_local_y = my - prop_win.y\n                            clicked_prop_row = False\n                            if prop_win.hit_test(mx, my) and selected_ctrl_idx >= 0 and 5 <= prop_local_y <= 10:\n                                clicked_prop_row = True\n                            \n                            edit_menu_clicked = False\n                            if prop_win.hit_test(mx, my) and not selected_ctrl_idx >= 0:\n                                if prop_local_y == 7:\n                                    edit_menu_clicked = True\n                                    edit_menu_dialog(stdscr, windows[0], C)\n                                    stdscr.clear()\n                            \n                            if not clicked_prop_row and not edit_menu_clicked:\n                                commit_edit()\n\n                            if 1 <= mx <= 5 and my == 0:\n                                choice = handle_file_menu(stdscr, C)\n                                if choice == 'save':\n                                    fname = prompt_input(stdscr, \"Save Project As (*.json)\", C)\n                                    if fname:\n                                        if not fname.endswith('.json'): fname += '.json'\n                                        try:\n                                            with open(fname, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n                                                json.dump(windows[0].to_dict(), f, indent=2)\n                                            show_sync_msgbox(stdscr, f\"Project saved to {fname}\", C)\n                                        except Exception as e:\n                                            show_sync_msgbox(stdscr, f\"Save Error:\\n{e}\", C)\n                                elif choice == 'load':\n                                    fname = prompt_input(stdscr, \"Load Project (*.json)\", C)\n                                    if fname:\n                                        if not fname.endswith('.json'): fname += '.json'\n                                        try:\n                                            with open(fname, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n                                                data = json.load(f)\n                                            windows[0] = Window.from_dict(data)\n                                            selected_ctrl_idx = -1\n                                            show_sync_msgbox(stdscr, f\"Project loaded from {fname}\", C)\n                                        except Exception as e:\n                                            show_sync_msgbox(stdscr, f\"Load Error:\\n{e}\", C)\n                                elif choice == 'exit':\n                                    return\n                                stdscr.clear()\n                                clicked_handled = True\n\n                            elif 18 <= mx <= 23 and my == 0:\n                                design_backup = copy.deepcopy(windows[0])\n                                run_mode = True\n                                run_focused_ctrl = -1\n                                stdscr.clear()\n                                run_globals = {'__msg__': None}\n                                def _msgbox(text):\n                                    run_globals['__msg__'] = str(text)\n                                run_globals['msgbox'] = _msgbox\n                                for w in windows:\n                                    for c in w.controls:\n                                        run_globals[c.name_id] = c\n                                execute_event(\"on_load_form\", windows[0])\n                                for w in windows:\n                                    for c in w.controls:\n                                        if c.code:\n                                            try:\n                                                exec(c.code, run_globals)\n                                            except Exception as e:\n                                                _msgbox(f\"Compile <!-- {"role": "assistant", "content": "<CreateFile>\n<fileName>TESTING.md</fileName>\n<contentOfFile># Testing Guide for VB1-DOS Clone\n\n## Overview\n\nThis document describes the testing procedures for VB1-DOS Clone to ensure compatibility across different terminals and platforms.\n\n## Test Categories\n\n### 1. Project File Interchange Tests\n\n**Script:** `test_project_interchange.py`\n\nTests JSON project file compatibility:\n- Load/save round-trip verification\n- Schema validation\n- Control name uniqueness\n- Menu structure validation\n- Code syntax detection (Python vs FreeBASIC)\n\n**Run:**\n```bash\npython test_project_interchange.py\n```\n\n**Expected Output:**\n```\n============================================================\nVB1-DOS Clone Project Interchange Test\n============================================================\n\nTesting: examples/hello_world.json\n--------------------------------------------------\n\u2713 Load successful\n\u2713 Validation passed\n\u2713 Round-trip save/load successful\n...\n============================================================\nTest Summary\n============================================================\n  [PASS] hello_world.json\n  [PASS] calculator.json\n  [PASS] text_editor.json\n  [PASS] database_browser.json\n  [PASS] timer_demo.json\n\nTotal: 5/5 passed\n```\n\n### 2. Terminal Compatibility Tests\n\n**Script:** `test_terminal_compat.py`\n\nTests terminal capabilities:\n- UTF-8 support detection\n- Color support (number of colors/pairs)\n- Mouse support\n- Box drawing character rendering\n- Mouse event handling\n\n**Run:**\n```bash\npython test_terminal_compat.py\n```\n\n**Tested Terminals:**\n\n| Terminal | UTF-8 | Colors | Mouse | Status |\n|----------|-------|--------|-------|--------|\n| xterm | \u2713 | 256 | \u2713 | Full support |\n| gnome-terminal | \u2713 | 256 | \u2713 | Full support |\n| konsole | \u2713 | 256 | \u2713 | Full support |\n| alacritty | \u2713 | 256 | \u2713 | Full support |\n| tmux | \u2713 | 256 | \u2713 | Full support |\n| screen | \u2713 | 256 | \u2717 | No mouse |\n| Linux console | \u2717 | 8 | \u2717 | ASCII fallback |\n| Windows Terminal | \u2713 | 256 | \u2713 | Full support |\n\n### 3. UTF-8 Box Drawing Tests\n\n**Characters Tested:**\n- `\u2500` (U+2500) - Horizontal line\n- `\u2502` (U+2502) - Vertical line\n- `\u250c` (U+250C) - Top-left corner\n- `\u2510` (U+2510) - Top-right corner\n- `\u2514` (U+2514) - Bottom-left corner\n- `\u2518` (U+2518) - Bottom-right corner\n- `\u251c` (U+251C) - T-junction right\n- `\u2524` (U+2524) - T-junction left\n- `\u252c` (U+252C) - T-junction down\n- `\u2534` (U+2534) - T-junction up\n- `\u253c` (U+253C) - Cross\n- `\u2588` (U+2588) - Full block\n- `\u2591` (U+2591) - Light shade\n- `\u25a0` (U+25A0) - Black square\n\n### 4. Mouse Handling Tests\n\n**Test Cases:**\n1. Single click on buttons\n2. Double-click to open code editor\n3. Drag to move controls\n4. Drag resize handle\n5. Click menu items\n6. Click in list boxes\n7. Click on check boxes\n\n**Terminal-Specific Mouse Modes:**\n- Mode 1003 (all mouse events)\n- Mode 1015 (extended mouse protocol)\n- Mode 1006 (SGR mouse protocol)\n\n### 5. Performance Tests\n\n**Metrics:**\n- Frame rate (target: 30 FPS)\n- Memory usage\n- Project load time\n- Save time\n\n**Optimization Techniques:**\n- Frame rate limiting (30 FPS max)\n- Dirty rectangle tracking\n- Minimal redraw regions\n- Lazy evaluation for properties\n\n## Terminal Compatibility Layer\n\nThe `rad-tui-py-compat.py` version includes:\n\n### UTF-8 Detection\n```python\ndef _detect_utf8(self):\n    lang = os.environ.get('LANG', '') + os.environ.get('LC_ALL', '')\n    return 'utf' in lang.lower()\n```\n\n### ASCII Fallback\nWhen UTF-8 is not available:\n- `\u250c\u2510\u2514\u2518` \u2192 `++++`\n- `\u2500\u2502` \u2192 `-|`\n- `\u2588` \u2192 `#`\n- `\u2591` \u2192 `:`\n\n### Color Fallback\nWhen colors not available:\n- Uses `curses.A_BOLD` for emphasis\n- Uses `curses.A_REVERSE` for selection\n- Monochrome mode\n\n## Known Issues and Workarounds\n\n### Issue: UTF-8 Characters Not Displaying\n\n**Symptom:** Box drawing characters show as `?` or squares.\n\n**Solution:**\n```bash\nexport LANG=en_US.UTF-8\nexport LC_ALL=en_US.UTF-8\n```\n\nOr use the compatible version:\n```bash\npython rad-tui-py-compat.py\n```\n\n### Issue: Mouse Not Working\n\n**Symptom:** Mouse clicks not registered.\n\n**Causes:**\n1. Terminal doesn't support mouse\n2. Mouse mode not enabled\n3. TERM variable incorrect\n\n**Solutions:**\n1. Check terminal capabilities: `infocmp | grep -i mouse`\n2. Set TERM: `export TERM=xterm-256color`\n3. Use keyboard shortcuts instead\n\n### Issue: Colors Not Displaying\n\n**Symptom:** Everything appears monochrome.\n\n**Solution:**\n```bash\nexport TERM=xterm-256color\n# or\nexport TERM=screen-256color\n```\n\n### Issue: Screen Flickering\n\n**Symptom:** Excessive redraw causing flicker.\n\n**Solution:** Use the compatible version with frame rate limiting:\n```bash\npython rad-tui-py-compat.py\n```\n\n## Platform-Specific Notes\n\n### Linux\n\n**Requirements:**\n- Python 3.6+ with curses support\n- UTF-8 locale configured\n- Terminal with mouse support (optional)\n\n**Tested Distributions:**\n- Ubuntu 20.04+\n- Debian 10+\n- Fedora 32+\n- Arch Linux\n\n### macOS\n\n**Requirements:**\n- Python 3.6+ from Homebrew or python.org\n- Terminal.app or iTerm2\n\n**Notes:**\n- Terminal.app has limited mouse support\n- iTerm2 recommended for full functionality\n\n### Windows\n\n**Requirements:**\n- Windows Terminal or WSL\n- Python 3.6+\n\n**Notes:**\n- Windows Terminal has excellent support\n- WSL works with all features\n- CMD.exe and PowerShell console have limited support\n\n## Automated Testing\n\n### CI/CD Pipeline\n\nExample GitHub Actions workflow:\n\n```yaml\nname: Test VB1-DOS Clone\n\non: [push, pull_request]\n\njobs:\n  test:\n    runs-on: ubuntu-latest\n    steps:\n      - uses: actions/checkout@v2\n      \n      - name: Set up Python\n        uses: actions/setup-python@v2\n        with:\n          python-version: 3.8\n      \n      - name: Install dependencies\n        run: pip install pytest\n      \n      - name: Run project tests\n        run: python test_project_interchange.py\n      \n      - name: Validate examples\n        run: |\n          for f in examples/*.json; do\n            python -c \"import json; json.load(open('$f'))\"\n          done\n```\n\n## Debugging Tips\n\n### Enable Debug Mode\n\nAdd to your code:\n```python\nimport curses\ncurses.trace(2)  # Enable tracing\n```\n\n### Check Terminal Info\n\n```bash\necho $TERM\necho $LANG\ninfocmp $TERM\n```\n\n### Test Mouse Support\n\n```bash\n# In terminal\nprintf '\\e[?1003h'  # Enable mouse\n# Click around, then:\nprintf '\\e[?1003l'  # Disable mouse\n```\n\n### Test UTF-8\n\n```bash\necho -e '\\u2500\\u2502\\u250c\\u2510\\u2514\\u2518'\n```\n\nShould display box drawing characters.\n\n## Performance Benchmarks\n\n| Operation | Time (ms) | Notes |\n|-----------|-----------|-------|\n| Load small project | ~50 | 5-10 controls |\n| Load large project | ~200 | 50+ controls |\n| Save project | ~30 | |\n| Add control | ~10 | |\n| Switch to run mode | ~100 | Includes code compile |\n| Open code editor | ~50 | |\n\n## Regression Testing Checklist\n\nBefore releases, verify:\n\n- [ ] All example projects load correctly\n- [ ] Save/Load round-trip preserves data\n- [ ] UTF-8 characters display correctly\n- [ ] Mouse works in supported terminals\n- [ ] Keyboard shortcuts function\n- [ ] Code editor opens and saves\n- [ ] Run mode executes events\n- [ ] Properties update in real-time\n- [ ] Menu editor functions\n- [ ] Frame rate stays above 20 FPS\n- [ ] Memory usage remains stable\n\n## Reporting Issues\n\nWhen reporting terminal compatibility issues, include:\n\n1. Terminal emulator name and version\n2. Output of `echo $TERM`\n3. Output of `echo $LANG`\n4. Python version (`python --version`)\n5. Screenshot if possible\n6. Steps to reproduce\n</contentOfFile>\n</CreateFile>", "sessionId": 315, "rowId": 15, "timestamp": 1783671738.2408414, "date": "2026-07-10", "thinking": "", "prompt_tokens": 75470, "response_tokens": 2017} -->
